(1) **New module-level `SAT_ART` table** (placed just above `class DebrisSatellite`): **six original, wrecked satellite silhouettes** ‚Äî comms bus + twin solar panels (right panel snapped/skewed), dish relay (drooping/cracked parabolic dish), boxy Earth-observer with an instrument boom (one panel hanging broken), a Sputnik-ish sphere with radial whip antennas (one bent), a cylindrical spent upper-stage/booster (dented skin, flared nozzle), and a truss/array segment (one rail snapped short, torn end cap). Each entry is `{ full, small }`, where each of those is an array of `{ pts, closed }` polylines authored in **unit space** (every coord inside the radius-1 circle so it scales cleanly to any tier by √ó`this.radius`), drawn through the **existing `drawPoly`/`glowStroke`** at `COLOR.debris` ‚Äî **no fills, no new render primitive, no external assets** (original stylized art authored in code, nothing traced/imported ‚Äî FLAG A-7; the file stays a self-contained GPL-3.0 HTML). (2) **`DebrisSatellite` rewired** ‚Äî the constructor now picks one archetype per instance (`this.art = SAT_ART[floor(rand(0, SAT_ART.length))]`; splits re-roll independently since each `new DebrisSatellite(...)` re-runs the ctor), selects the `small` variant at the small tier (`size === 1`) else `full`, and **bakes a per-instance copy ONCE** ‚Äî each polyline's points scaled to `this.radius` with a small random per-vertex jitter (`0.045¬∑radius` px) for a "no two alike / wrecked" look ‚Äî into `this.art`. The old procedural `this.hull` + `this.shards` fields are **gone**; `draw()` just iterates `this.art` (`for (const pl of this.art) drawPoly(pl.pts, this.x, this.y, this.angle, COLOR.debris, pl.closed)`). Jitter is applied in the ctor, **never per frame**. (3) **Random spawn rotation preserved (item 5)** ‚Äî `this.angle = rand(0, TAU)` and `this.spin = rand(-1.2, 1.2)` survive the draw-path rewrite; nothing anchors art to a fixed "up" (the draw path only rotates by `this.angle`, which `update()` advances by `this.spin`). Asserted with a 40-instance spread. (4) **Small-tier legibility gate** ‚Äî at `radius = 13` a 10+ segment design is mush, so each archetype's `small` variant is a simplified 2‚Äì4 stroke reduction (body + one feature); the small tier draws it instead of `full`. A look-call, tuned by eye. (5) **Collision unchanged** ‚Äî `this.radius`/`DEBRIS_RADII` are untouched; art is cosmetic, collision stays a circle (GDD ¬ß3.1). The title screen's decorative `titleDebris` uses `DebrisSatellite`, so it gets the new art for free. **Headless-tested** (`scratchpad/test-v33-p2.js`, new, **28 assertions**, driving the REAL class + table ‚Äî no reimplementation): `SAT_ART` is 5‚Äì6 entries, every `full`/`small` an array of `{ pts:[[x,y]‚Ä¶], closed:bool }` with **every unit-space coord inside the radius-1 circle** (caught one truss corner at magnitude 1.007 and pulled it in); a fresh `DebrisSatellite` of each size has a non-empty baked `art`, a random `angle` in `[0,TAU)` and `spin` in `[-1.2,1.2]`, unchanged collision `radius`; a 40-instance spread confirms `angle` is per-instance random (not anchored) and `spin` tumbles both ways; `draw()` is crash-free at all three sizes; each archetype's `small` variant is ‚â§ its `full` in polyline count; per-instance jitter makes instances differ and the baked `art` is a copy, not the shared `SAT_ART` reference; `hull`/`shards` are gone. **Also hardened `test-firerate.js`** ‚Äî its section D counts fire-cadence volleys over 1 s of real `update()` but didn't clear ambient hazards, so a wave-1 debris/saucer drifting into the stationary test ship could land a hit whose hit-stun interrupts firing and drops the volley count below the expected band ‚Äî a **pre-existing** rare RNG-timing flake (~0.7% on HEAD, same class as the documented `test-p5`/`test-starfield` flakes) whose rate rides on the shared `Math.random` sequence, so P2's extra per-instance ctor `rand()` calls lifted it to ~4%. The fix clears `game.debris`/`hunters`/`saucers` each frame **exactly as it already clears `game.bullets`** ‚Äî the test's own stated intent (its comments) is to isolate *cooldown-driven* cadence ‚Äî taking it from 6/150 to **0/250** flakes; **no game logic changed** (verified: HEAD flaked too, and my change only reshuffles RNG, not the fire code). **Full regression re-run green: all 20 test files, 916 assertions** (up from 888 ‚Äî the new file adds 28; no other existing test needed a change beyond the firerate isolation hardening). `node --check` clean on the extracted script. (1) **Rename** ‚Äî "Asteroid Field Deluxe" ‚Üí **"Orbital Overhaul"** everywhere: the `<title>` tag, the header banner comment's first line (version-log body kept as-is), the title screen (`"ASTEROID FIELD"`/`"D E L U X E"` ‚Üí `"ORBITAL"`/`"O V E R H A U L"`, same sizes/colors/positions), and the doc set ‚Äî `asteroid-field-deluxe-GDD.md` ‚Üí **`orbital-overhaul-GDD.md`** (git-mv'd, H1 + Version line updated), `CLAUDE.md`'s doc-layer pointer, and this file's own H1 + design-authority reference. **The two `localStorage` keys (`afd_settings_v1`, `afd_achievements_v2`) are deliberately NOT renamed** ‚Äî the `afd_` prefix is load-bearing (renaming either wipes every player's saved settings/bindings/achievement tiers on next load); an in-code comment now sits at each declaration saying so. (3) **Clump silhouette** ‚Äî in `Garbage.draw()`, `pieces > 1` now takes a completely different branch from `pieces === 1` (unchanged, byte-identical): ONE closed hull polygon (7‚Äì9 vertices jittered around the derived `radius = 7¬∑‚àöpieces`) replaces the v3.2 P1 mini-canister cluster, because playtest read the cluster as "a pile of pickups" rather than "a target." A new `makeClumpHull(radius)` helper generates the hull **once**, cached on `this.hull` ‚Äî set in the constructor, regenerated only at merge time inside `coalesceGarbage` (never per frame) ‚Äî and rotated live by `this.spin` so it still tumbles. Changes: (1) **Decay removed entirely** ‚Äî the `decay` field, the `GARBAGE_DECAY` (12 s) / `GARBAGE_SEVER_DECAY` (10 s) constants, the decay countdown + death in `Garbage.update()`, the blink-out branch in `Garbage.draw()`, and the `game.stats.garbageDecayed` increment are all gone; `Garbage`'s ctor dropped its `decay` param (mass is now the 5th arg) and `Garbage.fromNode` dropped its `decay` param. A canister now leaves the field by exactly **two doors: RECYCLED or CONSUMED INTO A HUNTER** ‚Äî never by aging out. (Powerup decay is a separate system ‚Äî untouched.) (2) **Economy closed (FORK-B / B1)** ‚Äî the coalescence transform site tags its new core `bornOfScrap = true`; `HunterSatellite` gained a `bornOfScrap` field (default `false`); `destroyHunter` propagates the flag to the 3 split children (both generations) and **skips ALL garbage emission for a `bornOfScrap` Hunter at every tier** (large/medium 3-normal burst AND the small-tier 6-low-mass burst). Score, splits, contact damage, and the small-tier powerup drop are **unchanged** ‚Äî only the garbage emission is suppressed. Rationale: with decay gone, a normal 13-member lineage drops `12 + 54 = 66` canisters, so an un-suppressed scrap-born lineage would be a **5.5√ó amplifier** (12 pieces in ‚Üí 66 out) and the field would diverge without bound; B1 makes it **12 in, 0 out** (that scrap has already been spent ‚Äî it IS the Hunter now), and gives the player a real reason to *let* a clump transform occasionally (a scrap-born lineage is pure score, no cleanup bill). Timer-spawned Hunters (`bornOfScrap = false`) are untouched and still drop the full 66. (3) **Two constants retuned** (both commented as playtest knobs): `GARBAGE_COALESCE_DELAY` **1.0 ‚Üí 6.0 s** (at the 20‚Äì55 px/s emission kick, 6 s carries same-explosion siblings 120‚Äì330 px apart, so a burst drifts apart and *later happens upon strangers* instead of instantly re-clumping ‚Äî Phase 2's shatter path reuses this same constant, one knob); `GARBAGE_MAGNET_RANGE` **140 ‚Üí 260 px** (140 was tuned when garbage lived 12 s and only had to find siblings in a fresh tight cloud; with permanent garbage, pieces that drift further apart would never re-find each other and the field would silt up ‚Äî flagged in-code as the first thing to tune by feel, FLAG D-1). (4) **"Waste Not" repurposed in place** ‚Äî id + pool slot kept (so the 16-entry weekly pool length, `poolIndex` rotation math, and `test-f9`'s hardcoded slice values need NO recompute); new per-game stat `game.stats.hunterCoalesced` (incremented once at the coalescence transform, replacing the removed `garbageDecayed`); desc + `cur()` rewritten to `(s.gameEnded && s.hunterCoalesced === 0)` ‚Äî "finish a game with no Hunters born from neglected scrap." Kept the display name (it still fits: you wasted no salvage to the coalescence sink). **Did NOT** (per the phase's explicit non-scope): add a spatial hash to `coalesceGarbage` (O(n¬≤) with the early-continue is fine at realistic counts, render is viewport-culled ‚Äî follow-up only if a stress test shows it, FLAG D-2); change `DEBRIS_GARBAGE`/`HUNTER_GARBAGE`/`HUNTER_SMALL_GARBAGE` (held in reserve as playtest levers); or touch `GARBAGE_CLUMP_MAXSPD`. **Headless-tested** ‚Äî `scratchpad/test-v31-coalesce.js` extended 61 ‚Üí **80 assertions** and `scratchpad/test-f9.js` 277 ‚Üí **283**, both driving the REAL `update`/`destroyHunter`/`coalesceGarbage`/`evaluate` (no reimplementation): a canister survives a ~120 s `update()` run and never dies of age; `garbageDecayed` is gone from `game.stats`; a `bornOfScrap` core killed through its FULL lineage (large ‚Üí 3 med ‚Üí 9 small, 13 kills) emits **ZERO** garbage while awarding the **same** score (2900) as a normal lineage and still dropping its small-tier powerup (RNG-forced, 9/9); a **timer-spawned** Hunter still emits the full **12 normal + 54 low = 66**; the `bornOfScrap` flag survives **both** split generations; `hunterCoalesced` increments exactly once per 12-piece transform; the constant retunes are asserted (6.0 / 260) and section (1)'s delay-gate test was reworked to advance past the 6 s delay via the constant; Waste Not unlocks on a zero-coalescence finished game and does NOT unlock after one Hunter is born from scrap; the weekly pool is still length 16 with every `poolIndex` assertion **unchanged**. `test-f3.js` adjusted (dropped the two removed constants from its symbol list, moved mass to the 5th ctor arg, and swapped the sever-decay assertion for a "severed garbage carries no `decay` field" check). **Full regression re-run green: all 18 test files, 872 assertions** (up from 847 ‚Äî coalesce +19, f9 +6; `node --check` clean on the extracted script). GDD updated in place: **¬ß2.10** "Garbage drops" + "Chain vulnerability" (canisters no longer decay / severed scrap no longer gets a shorter decay), **¬ß2.10.1** ‚Äî the load-bearing "Decay exists to protect readability ‚Äî don't remove it" bullet **rewritten** to say coalescence + shatter-to-harvest are the new density levers, *with the reason the old rationale was superseded so a future session doesn't restore it*, **¬ß2.5.1** (the `bornOfScrap` rule + rationale, the 6.0 s delay, the 260 px range, the two-exits framing), **¬ß2.17** (repurposed Waste Not), plus the top Version line, Architecture Map (Constants / Entity classes / game-object / Flow-functions / update(dt) rows), the ¬ß2.4/¬ß2.7/¬ß4-roadmap/perf-risk/playtest-ask mentions of decay-as-a-lever, and a new ¬ß7 Version History v3.2 P3 entry. Did NOT push. **Next up per `IMPLEMENTATION-PHASES-v3.2.md`:** whatever Phase 4+ scopes (v3.2 is Phase 3 of N); the round's playtest asks (magnet range, coalesce delay, shatter-loop engagement, clump heft/legibility, late-wave perf, B1-as-a-real-choice) are logged below for the next round. ‚öÝÔ∏è **Prior session: v3.2 Phase 2 ‚Äî shatter a clump with one shot.** Phase 1 made a `pieces>1` clump un-hookable; this phase is the tool that reopens it. Changes: (1) **New collision branch** ‚Äî in the non-hostile bullet loop, alongside the existing debris/saucer/hunter branches, a player bullet is now tested against every `pieces > 1` clump (`dist2` against the clump's P1-derived `radius`); on a hit `b.dead = true` and `shatterClump(g)` fires, then `break`. A `pieces === 1` single is still **not** a bullet target ‚Äî player bullets pass straight through it exactly as before ‚Äî and hostile (saucer) bullets still pass through **all** garbage regardless of `pieces` (untouched hostile branch). (2) **New flow function `shatterClump(g)`**, placed right after `destroyHunter` (shaped like `destroyDebris`/`destroyHunter` ‚Äî a flow function, not a method): `g.dead = true`; a small `boom(g.x, g.y, 1, COLOR.garbage)` for the pop; then exactly `g.pieces` fresh `new Garbage(...)` singles pushed at `(g.x, g.y)`, each getting `mass = g.mass / g.pieces` (per-piece mass identity from mixed merges is averaged back out ‚Äî FLAG A-3, an accepted, invisible-in-play fidelity trade), the constructor's default `pieces = 1` + **full, re-armed `coalesceDelay`** (no special-casing needed ‚Äî `new Garbage()` already starts at `pieces=1` and a full delay), and an outward kick of `rand(GARBAGE_SHATTER_KICK[0], GARBAGE_SHATTER_KICK[1])` px/s added to `0.25√ó` the clump's own drift, mirroring the `destroyDebris` fan-out pattern exactly. **No score** ‚Äî `addScore()` is deliberately not called; the reward is the newly-hookable canisters themselves. (3) **New constant `GARBAGE_SHATTER_KICK = [40, 90]`** (px/s outward-kick range), added to the salvage/chain constants block next to the other `GARBAGE_*` values, commented as a playtest knob. Did NOT touch decay, emission counts, the coalescence pass itself, or the Hunter transform (Phase 3 owns those). **Headless-tested** (`scratchpad/test-v31-coalesce.js` extended 48‚Üí**61 assertions** ‚Äî drives the REAL bullet loop / `update()`/`shatterClump`, no reimplementation; `Bullet` and `shatterClump` added to the test harness's returned-symbol list): one player bullet on a `pieces=7` clump (mass 3.5) yields exactly 7 live singles, all `pieces===1`, all with a full re-armed `coalesceDelay`, all `mass === clumpMass/7` (0.5), total emitted mass conserves the clump's mass exactly, and `game.stats.garbageDecayed` is untouched by the shatter; those 7 do **not** immediately re-merge on the very next `update()` frame (the 1 s delay gate holds); a player bullet passes straight **through** a `pieces=1` canister (neither dies); a hostile bullet passes straight through a `pieces=6` clump (clump survives); and ‚Äî the point of the whole phase ‚Äî the 7 emitted pieces **are** hookable once in pickup range: shattering a `pieces=3` clump sitting on the ship, then driving one further real `update()` frame, hooks all 3 resulting singles onto the chain (the P1 `pieces===1` pickup gate now lets them through). Version line + a new ¬ß7 Version History v3.2 P2 entry (appended to the existing P1 entry) also updated. **Next up per `IMPLEMENTATION-PHASES-v3.2.md`: Phase 3 ‚Äî garbage never decays + close the escalation loop** (removing `GARBAGE_DECAY`/`GARBAGE_SEVER_DECAY`, the `bornOfScrap` no-garbage-emission rule for coalescence-born Hunters per FORK-B/B1, retuning `GARBAGE_COALESCE_DELAY` 1.0‚Üí6.0 and `GARBAGE_MAGNET_RANGE` 140‚Üí260, and repurposing the "Waste Not" achievement in place). ‚öÝÔ∏è **Prior session: v3.2 Phase 1 ‚Äî garbage clumps gain real mass, size, and a cluster silhouette; clumps are now un-hookable.** Reverses the shipped v3.1 **FORK-2** decision (GDD ¬ß2.5.1): FORK-2 kept a clump's mass at 1.0 so it towed as one normal canister ‚Äî correct *only while clumps were hookable*. This phase makes clumps un-hookable, removing FORK-2's reason. Changes, all in `coalesceGarbage`/`Garbage`/the pickup pass: (1) **`Garbage.mass` SUMS on merge** ‚Äî the survivor takes `a.mass + b.mass` (was: kept its base mass); `pieces` keeps its meaning (the 1..11 threat counter, Hunter at 12). (2) **`Garbage.radius` is derived** ‚Äî `7 * Math.sqrt(this.pieces)`, recomputed in the constructor and at every merge (a single piece still reads 7 ‚Äî no new constant). (3) **Merge velocity is now momentum-conserving** ‚Äî `v = (a.mass*a.v + b.mass*b.v)/(a.mass+b.mass)` with the PRE-merge masses, replacing the shipped literal vector sum (with mass summing + garbage soon permanent, a literal sum made every merge ADD speed ‚Üí clumps became the fastest things on screen). (4) **Attraction is mass-weighted** ‚Äî `a.v += (dx/d)*GARBAGE_MAGNET_PULL*b.mass*dt`, `b.v -= (dx/d)*GARBAGE_MAGNET_PULL*a.mass*dt` (gravity-like, momentum-conserving; reduces EXACTLY to the shipped symmetric pull at mass 1.0, so `GARBAGE_MAGNET_PULL` is unretuned) ‚Äî heavy clumps become slow anchors loose singles fall into. The wrap-aware `dist2`/`shortDelta` math and the off-by-default `GARBAGE_CLUMP_MAXSPD` clamp are untouched. (5) **Cluster render** ‚Äî `Garbage.draw()` at `pieces>1` draws `pieces` mini-canisters via the existing `drawCanister` at golden-angle offsets (`theta = k*2.39996`, `r = 5*sqrt(k)` for `k` in `0..pieces-1`), all rotated by `this.spin` so the wad tumbles as one body; `pieces===1` collapses to a single centered canister, byte-identical to before; the `mass<1` paler-tint rule kept. (6) **A clump cannot be towed** ‚Äî the pickup hook now additionally requires `g.pieces === 1` (the load-bearing rule; the next phase adds the shatter tool), and the **Magnet powerup pull also skips `pieces>1`**. (7) Clumps stay **non-solid** to the ship (FORK-A2 ‚Äî zero contact damage, not added to `hazards`; hazard loop untouched). Did NOT touch decay, bullet collision, shatter, or emission counts (those are Phases 2/3). **Headless-tested** (`scratchpad/test-v31-coalesce.js` extended 29‚Üí**48 assertions** ‚Äî drives the REAL `coalesceGarbage`/`update`/`Garbage`, no reimplementation): the old exact-vector-sum assertion was **rewritten** to the momentum sum (not deleted); mass sums across a chain of merges; radius tracks `7*sqrt(pieces)`; a heavy clump absorbing a fast light piece barely speeds up (momentum, 100‚Üí9.09); two mass-1.0 singles attract bit-identically to the shipped force (reduction guard); a `pieces>1` clump on the ship is NOT hooked while a `pieces=1` canister still hooks + is pulled; the Magnet won't pull a clump; `draw()` crash-free at `pieces=1` and `pieces=11`. No new constant added. **Next up per `IMPLEMENTATION-PHASES-v3.2.md`: Phase 2 ‚Äî shatter a clump with one shot** (the tool that makes un-hookable a game, not a wall) ‚Äî then Phase 3 (garbage never decays + close the escalation loop). ‚öÝÔ∏è **Prior session: v3.1 Phase 3 ‚Äî mutual garbage magnetism + coalescence ‚Üí Hunter formation.** Uncollected salvage is now a *threat*, not just decaying scrap. Added a per-frame **`coalesceGarbage(dt)`** pass (defined just before `updateChain`, called in `update()` immediately after the garbage pickup/magnet loop and before `updateChain(dt)`). Every `Garbage` gained two constructor defaults ‚Äî **`coalesceDelay = GARBAGE_COALESCE_DELAY` (1.0 s)** and **`pieces = 1`** ‚Äî inherited by all three emission sites (`destroyDebris`, `destroyHunter` large/medium, `destroyHunter` small) **and** `Garbage.fromNode`; `coalesceDelay` counts down in `Garbage.update()`, and a piece is **active** once it's ‚â§ 0. `coalesceGarbage` is O(n¬≤) over active pieces (skipping any already dead this pass), all wrap-aware (`dist2`/`shortDelta`): **both** attraction and merging require **both** pieces active, so a fresh burst rides its explosion kick apart for 1 s before it can clump. *Attraction:* each active pair within `GARBAGE_MAGNET_RANGE` (140) accelerates toward the other at `GARBAGE_MAGNET_PULL` (40 px/s¬≤), symmetric (equal & opposite); an off-by-default `GARBAGE_CLUMP_MAXSPD` (Infinity) speed clamp is a playtest knob (applied only in the attraction branch, via a `clampGarbageSpeed` helper ‚Äî kept out of the merge path so the literal-vector-sum contract stays exact). *Merge* (both active, `dist2 < GARBAGE_MERGE_DIST¬≤` = 12¬≤): survivor velocity becomes the **literal vector sum** (`survivor.vx += other.vx; vy += other.vy`), `survivor.pieces += other.pieces`, `other.dead = true`; the survivor keeps its **base mass** (FORK-2 ‚Äî a clump tows as one normal mass-1.0 canister, `pieces` is purely the threat trigger, decoupled from tow weight). A survivor stays in the inner loop after a merge (`continue`) so it can absorb multiple pieces in one pass ‚Äî twelve co-located pieces collapse in a single frame. *Transform:* at `survivor.pieces >= HUNTER_COALESCE_COUNT` (12), `survivor.dead = true`, `game.hunters.push(new HunterSatellite(x, y, 3))`, `AudioSys.hunterborn()`, and `break` (survivor is gone). Coalesced Hunters are **independent of `game.hunterTimer`** (FORK-1 ‚Äî multiple concurrent lineages allowed; the timed spawn stays one-at-a-time). **A merge does NOT increment `game.stats.garbageDecayed`** ‚Äî coalescing is a *distinct* fate from decaying and must not trip Waste Not (verified). Relies on the existing end-of-frame dead-filter (`game.garbage = game.garbage.filter(...)`) for compaction ‚Äî no new filter added. **Pickup (FORK-2) needed no change** ‚Äî the existing gate pushes one node per hooked piece, so a `pieces>1` clump hooks & delivers as one mass-1.0 node (confirmed via the real `update()`). **New `AudioSys.hunterborn()`** ‚Äî a distinct ominous cue on `this.sfx` (guarded `if (!this.ctx) return`): two low sawtooth voices, ~196‚Üí138 Hz and ~139‚Üí98 Hz (a dissonant ~‚àö2/tritone apart), both descending over ~0.4 s ‚Äî darker/longer than `explosion`; audio isn't spatialized so it plays whether the Hunter forms on- or off-screen (the only off-screen tell). **New constants** in the salvage/chain block near `GARBAGE_DECAY`: `GARBAGE_COALESCE_DELAY` (1.0), `GARBAGE_MAGNET_RANGE` (140), `GARBAGE_MAGNET_PULL` (40), `GARBAGE_MERGE_DIST` (12), `HUNTER_COALESCE_COUNT` (12), `GARBAGE_CLUMP_MAXSPD` (Infinity) ‚Äî all tunable. **Headless-tested** (`scratchpad/test-v31-coalesce.js`, 29 assertions, new ‚Äî drives the REAL `coalesceGarbage`/`update`/`destroyDebris`/`Garbage`): (0) constants sane + default-ctor/`fromNode`/real-`destroyDebris`-emission all inherit `pieces=1`+full delay; (1) no merge before 1 s (driven through the real `update()` countdown at 0 s and 0.6 s), merge after; (2) two active pieces in contact merge ‚Äî survivor velocity == exact vector sum, `pieces==2`, earlier piece is survivor; (3) twelve active pieces ‚Üí exactly one new large Hunter, all twelve dead, `hunterborn` stub fired exactly once; (4) a merge across the world x-seam (wrap-aware) with the sum-velocity preserved; (5) `garbageDecayed` unchanged by both a plain merge and a 12‚ÜíHunter transform; (6) a `pieces=5` clump on the ship hooks as exactly one mass-1.0 chain node via the real `update()`; (7) attraction is 1 s-gated too (fresh pieces feel no pull; active pieces get an equal-and-opposite pull). Regression green across f2‚Äìf9 + P4‚ÄìP6 (**760 assertions across 15 files**). **Prior session: v3.0 Phase 7 ‚Äî tiered achievements infrastructure + convert existing lifetime set (Part A, ¬ßA-1..A-3/A-5/A-7).** Added an optional ascending **`tiers:[bronze,silver,gold,titanium,platinum,diamond]`** ladder to a lifetime definition (replacing its single `goal`), with `TIER_NAMES` + a warm-metal‚Üíwhite-hot **`TIER_COLOR[]`** palette beside `COLOR` (FLAG A-1-a ‚Äî no teal/green/lime so a badge never reads as a Hunter/Debris/salvage tell; all six are look-call tunables). **`evaluate()`** now forks: single-goal entries (all 15 weekly + the 5 non-tiered lifetime) keep the F9 `cur >= goal` path; a tiered entry unlocks **every newly-crossed tier in one pass, ascending** (a big lifetime jump pops several toasts at once, each naming its tier ‚Äî "Recycling Magnate ‚Äî Gold"), persisting the **highest tier index reached per id** in a new **`lifetimeTiers{id:idx}`** map. **Converted the seven flagged lifetime achievements** to the exact ¬ßA-3 ladders: Recycling Magnate (1k‚Üí100k), Ghost Protocol (50‚Üí10k), Saucer Hunter (250‚Üí10k), Perfect Wave (5‚Üí500), Iron Hull (100‚Üí10k) ‚Äî all **SUM** ‚Äî plus the two **MAX / personal-best** ones (FLAG A-1-b): Master of the Field (`l.maxWave`, 5‚Üí100) and No Powerups Needed (**new `l.maxWaveNoPowerup`**, 2‚Üí29). The MAX counter is updated `Math.max(current, wave)` **at each `nextWave` wave-clear only while `game.stats.powerupsPicked === 0`**, so it records the deepest wave reached before *any* powerup and **freezes** for the rest of the game the moment one is picked. **Reworded The Long Haul** (`l.fullChains`, still non-tiered) to a **fixed ‚â•12-delivered-in-one-visit √ó10**, decoupled from the growing `game.cargoMax` (FLAG A-5-a / B-8-b) ‚Äî the dock hook already latches on the literal `deliveryCount === 12`, so only the desc + an in-code comment changed. **Viewer rewrite:** `drawAchRow` renders a tiered lifetime row as **one row** ‚Äî name + right-aligned **tier badge + progress-to-next** in the tier's colour ("Gold ¬∑ 12,431 ‚Üí 25,000"; "Diamond ‚úì MAX" at the top; "‚Äî ¬∑ 0 ‚Üí 1,000" pre-bronze), via new `tierIndex`/`tierStatusText` helpers + a locale-independent `fmtCommas`. **Persistence bumped to `afd_achievements_v2`** (new shape `{lifetime, lifetimeTiers{id:idx}, lifetimeUnlocked[non-tiered], weekly{key,unlocked[]}}`); on load, if only the old `_v1` key exists, its raw lifetime **counters** are kept and tiers + non-tiered unlocks **re-derive silently** via a new **`deriveLifetime()`** (no toast storm ‚Äî evaluate() then only toasts *new* crossings this session), old flat `_v1` unlock sets ignored (FLAG A-2 / A-2-a). `deriveLifetime()` also runs after every load so badges match counters before the first in-game `evaluate()`; a stale-low stored tier is advanced (never lowered) and a stored idx is clamped to the ladder length. **The module still observes, never drives ‚Äî `cur()` untouched.** Kept the `typeof`-guard + try/catch (a corrupt v2 payload can't crash `init`). **`test-f9.js` heavily rewritten** (62‚Üí**169 assertions**): per-tier boundary sweeps for all 7 ladders (threshold-1 stays on the prior tier, exact threshold advances one), an explicit cross-bronze-not-silver + a multi-tier jump firing three ascending tier-named toasts, both MAX counters driven through the **real `nextWave`** (incl. the freeze-on-powerup), a v2 tier round-trip, the `_v1‚Üí_v2` migration (keeps counters, re-derives tiers, silent), a stale-tier advance, and a corrupt-payload no-crash. Weekly rotation + all non-tiered/gameplay paths stay green. **Prior session: v3.0 Phase 6 ‚Äî tow-capacity progression + chain physics retune (B-8).** The fixed `CHAIN_MAX = 12` is gone, replaced by a runtime **`game.cargoMax`** that starts at **`CARGO_BASE` (12)** and **grows +1 per `CARGO_GROW_PER` (30) canisters recycled (delivered) in the current run**, bounded by **`CARGO_CAP_MAX` (20)** ‚Äî cap-growth FORK A-fork-2 resolved **per-delivery** (the on-pillar choice: capacity earned by engaging the salvage loop, not handed out by wave). The growth check sits at the dock-offload site right after the per-run `game.stats.delivered++`, computing `min(CARGO_CAP_MAX, CARGO_BASE + floor(delivered / CARGO_GROW_PER))`; since `delivered` climbs by 1 per canister the cap rises at most one step at a time, each bump pushing a brief **"TOW +1"** float. `startGame` resets `cargoMax` to base. The **pickup gate** (`game.chain.length < game.cargoMax`) and **HUD** (`CARGO n/{cargoMax}`) now read the runtime cap. **Part 2 ‚Äî the physics retune (the real work):** a naive m=20 chain under the old coefficients would be ~33% thrust / 50% top speed (the "broken, not heavy" zone GDD ¬ß2.10.1 warns about), so the mass-penalty coefficients were **softened in lock-step** ‚Äî `CARGO_THRUST` 0.10‚Üí**0.06**, `CARGO_MAXSPD` 0.05‚Üí**0.03**, `CARGO_MASS` (tug) 0.12‚Üí**0.07** ‚Äî solved so a *full chain at the new ceiling* (m=20) lands on the **old full-12 feel: 1/(1+20¬∑0.06)=45.5% thrust, 1/(1+20¬∑0.03)=62.5% top speed**, and the tug's 1.4 cap is reached at m‚âà20 (was m‚âà12). The per-node penalty therefore shrinks as the ceiling rises: a base-12 chain is now genuinely lighter (~58% thrust / ~74% top speed / 0.84 tug), leaving handling headroom to grow into. **Stability revalidation (the load-bearing risk):** the constraint loop's literal `3` became **`CHAIN_ITER` (4)**. A headless stress at 20 nodes (hard thrust-flips across a wrap, 900 frames) shows **no NaN, no velocity explosion, worst-case link stretch ‚âà4 px on a 20 px link** ‚Äî already stable at 3 iters (4.36 px), but 4 tightens the worst link (link 0, anchor‚Üíhead ‚Äî the tail doesn't sag) and restores the pre-B-8 margin ¬ß3.4 validated at 12/3. **FLAG B-8-a resolved:** Engine (halves effective mass) at 20 nodes behaves like plain 10 (headless-asserted), acceptable both with/without. **FLAG B-8-b (for the achievements phases):** Heavy Hauler / Freight Baron / The Long Haul must key on a **fixed ‚â•12** delivered-in-one-visit, NOT `game.cargoMax` ‚Äî the existing dock full-visit hook still keys on a literal `12` (`if (game.deliveryCount === 12)`), so it's already decoupled; the achievements-overhaul phases (7‚Äì9) must keep it fixed as the cap grows. **FLAG B-8-c (perf):** more towed nodes + higher canister volume = more `shadowBlur` in dense late waves ‚Äî a browser-only playtest watch (`GARBAGE_DECAY` + a glow toggle remain the levers). **Also fixed the long-standing `test-f3` Engine-drop flake** (its `resetShip` now zeroes `game.powerFx`, so a random Engine drop during a prior `update()` can't halve `chainMass` and fail the (D) mass-sum assertions ‚Äî 10/10 green now). New/changed constants all in the salvage/chain block: `CARGO_BASE`/`CARGO_CAP_MAX`/`CARGO_GROW_PER`/`CHAIN_ITER` added, `CARGO_THRUST`/`CARGO_MAXSPD`/`CARGO_MASS` retuned, `CHAIN_MAX` removed. **Prior session: v3.0 Phase 5 ‚Äî Difficulty Options screen + powerup expiry modes (B-4/B-5).** Added an **Options ‚Üí Difficulty** sub-screen with two opt-in mode toggles ‚Äî **shot powerups (Rapid + Triple) expire by Time | Shots**, **Magnet expires by Time | Pieces** ‚Äî plus the count-based expiry logic behind them. Both settings default to **`"time"`**, so *nothing changes for anyone until they opt in* (headless-verified: default reproduces the shipped timed behaviour exactly). Design: two persisted fields in `afd_settings_v1` (`shotPowerupMode`, `magnetMode`) on a new module-level **`settings`** object (additive ‚Äî an older save missing the keys keeps the default, a corrupt value is ignored on load; no schema bump). Count budgets live in a new **`game.powerBudget {rapid,triple,magnet}`** (reset in `startGame`, parallel to `powerFx`; Engine has no budget ‚Äî it's always timed, never configurable). The single new coupling point is **`powerActive(type)`** (+ **`powerMode(type)`**): every "is this effect live?" read ‚Äî the fire block's triple-fan branch and rapid-cadence line, `maxBullets()`, `chainMass()` (Engine), the Magnet pull, and the HUD ‚Äî now routes through it, so the two modes can never diverge (in time mode it reads `powerFx` seconds; in a count mode it reads `powerBudget` count). Decrements: **Rapid/Triple** each spend one **per trigger-pull** in the fire block (a Triple 3-fan is ONE pull; with both active both budgets tick once per pull and end **independently** ‚Äî FLAG B-4-b; decrement placed *after* the fan/cadence reads so the last pull is fully a rapid/triple pull); **Magnet** spends one **per canister hooked** at the pickup/hook site ‚Äî counted at the hook, not the pull, so a magnet that draws-then-hooks a piece spends once (FLAG B-5-a). `applyPowerup` sets the timer (time mode) *or* the budget (count mode), and a same-type pickup **refreshes to full** either way (never stacks) ‚Äî matching the shipped rule. HUD: the active-effect row now iterates `powerActive` and, in a count mode, draws the bar as `remaining/POWERUP_BUDGET[type]` with a numeric shots/pieces label beside it (one renderer, two data sources). Menu: `"Difficulty"` added to `MENU_OPTIONS` before `"Back"` (Controls stays idx 3, Achievements idx 4, Difficulty idx 5, Back idx 6 ‚Äî no F8/F9/P4 test broke since those key off labels/idx‚â§4); a `"difficulty"` sub-screen (`DIFFICULTY_ROWS` + `menuDifficulty`, drawn by `drawDifficulty`) mirrors `menuOptions`/`drawOptionsMenu` ‚Äî two ‚óÑ/‚ñ∫ toggle rows (‚óÑ = timed default, ‚ñ∫ = count variant) + Back, navigable through the existing `menuInput` dispatcher, persisting on each flip; left **structured to grow** (add a row to `DIFFICULTY_ROWS` + a switch case + a renderer row ‚Äî FLAG B-4-c). New constants in the Powerups block: `RAPID_SHOTS` (40), `TRIPLE_SHOTS` (30), `MAGNET_PIECES` (20) + a `POWERUP_BUDGET` lookup. **All four FLAGs resolved as recommended** (B-4-a default time; B-4-b independent per-pull budgets; B-4-c growable screen; B-5-a count-at-hook). **One documented edge case:** switching a mode mid-effect (via the pause Difficulty screen) makes that effect read the *other* counter, which is 0 unless refreshed ‚Äî so an active effect can appear to end on a mid-game mode flip; acceptable ("you changed the rules"), and `startGame` zeroes both so a mode-consistent game never sees staleness. Prior session: **v3.0 Phase 4 (revised) ‚Äî pause/menu reachable from any state, with the corrected control scheme (B-1/B-2).** **This SUPERSEDES the earlier B-1-a mapping** (Start‚Üímenu) that a playtest rejected; the previous P4 attempt was reset out and this started clean at the P3 commit. `openPause()` is now callable from `title`/`gameover` as well as `playing` (`update()` already skips the sim outside `playing`, so `game.paused` is safe in any state). The **root menu is context-aware**, keyed purely on `game.state`: `rootItems()` returns `MENU_ROOT_PLAY = ["Continue","Options","Quit"]` when playing, else `MENU_ROOT_SYS = ["Options","Achievements","Back"]` (the system menu). `menuRoot()` now dispatches **by label** so one handler serves both layouts. The **corrected control scheme, as shipped:** (1) controller **Start = session toggle** ‚Äî title/gameover ‚Üí START A GAME, playing ‚Üí OPEN PAUSE, paused ‚Üí DISMISS & RESUME (this was already wired correctly on the clean tree, left as-is). (2) Keyboard **"O"** and controller **B** OPEN the Options/Achievements system menu from title/gameover; **Back** closes the overlay ‚Üí underlying screen. "O" is a literal inline check in the keydown normal branch (not a binding-table entry). (3) Keyboard **ESC** pauses during play and backs out inside a menu: `bindings.pause.keys` is now `["escape"]` (**"P" retired ‚Äî FLAG P4-a resolved: retire**) and shares ESC with `bindings.back.keys`; `handleMenuKey` resolves **confirm‚Üíback‚Üípause** in order, so in-menu ESC matches `back` first (= back), and outside a menu the normal branch's pause-during-playing check makes ESC pause. (4) Controller **B is context-aware, mirroring ESC**: menu-open ‚Üí back; no menu on title/gameover ‚Üí open the system menu. (5) A/Enter still start a game. **FLAG P4-b (a single confirm can't both nav a menu AND start a game)** is guaranteed structurally: the gamepad normal branch is an **else-if chain** (Start > B > A, so same-frame B+A opens the menu without also starting), and both input handlers hit the menu-open context (which returns) before the title "press to start" line. New `game.menu.achReturn` (`"root"`|`"options"`) tracks which parent the Achievements viewer backs out to, since it now has two entry points (system root directly, or via Options). `drawMenu()` now also overlays the **title** (added inside the title block before its early `return`) and **gameover** (moved to draw *after* the GAME OVER text so the menu sits on top); `drawRootMenu` reads `rootItems()` and titles the panel "PAUSED" (play) / "MENU" (system). Title/gameover control hints updated (title: "PAUSE: ESC" and "OPTIONS / ACHIEVEMENTS: O (controller: B)"; gameover gained the same options hint). **This closes the long-standing "menu / achievements reachable only via pause" limitation** flagged since F8/F9. Prior session: **v3.0 Phase 3 ‚Äî "targets remaining" HUD (B-7).** Added a `TARGETS n` readout directly under `CARGO` (`draw()`, HUD block), where `n = game.debris.length + game.hunters.length` ‚Äî literally the wave-clear gate one line below it in `update()` (`if (game.debris.length === 0 && game.hunters.length === 0)`), so `TARGETS 0` means the wave is about to clear. Went with the single-line `TARGETS n` form recommended in `PLANNED-FEATURES-v3.md` B-7 (not the two-part `DEBRIS n ¬∑ HUNTERS m` fallback) ‚Äî flagged for a playtest read on whether the count jump reads clearly. Lit (`COLOR.text`) while `n > 0`, dim otherwise, same convention as CARGO. No sim changes ‚Äî purely a HUD read of two existing array lengths. The active-powerup row shifted down 20px (`prow` 130‚Üí150) to make room for the new line. Documented in-code and in STATUS/GDD that the count can **rise** mid-wave: a Debris split (large ‚Üí 3 mediums, +2, FLAG B-7-a) or a Hunter lineage arriving on its own 14‚Äì32s timer from wave 2 on (FLAG B-7-b) ‚Äî intentional, not a bug, since the wave genuinely isn't over until Hunters clear too. Prior session: **v3.0 Phase 2 ‚Äî fire-rate rebalance (B-6).** A single `FIRE_COOLDOWN` (0.16 s) previously gated every shot, and Rapid Fire only raised `maxBullets()` ‚Äî cadence never changed, the bug Paul felt. (1) Base `FIRE_COOLDOWN` retuned slower, 0.16‚Üí0.20 s. (2) New `RAPID_FIRE_COOLDOWN` (0.09 s), clearly faster than base. (3) The fire block in `Ship.update` now sets its post-shot cooldown to `RAPID_FIRE_COOLDOWN` when `game.powerFx.rapid > 0`, else `FIRE_COOLDOWN`. Triple Shot is untouched ‚Äî it still fires the 3-bullet spread on the base cadence and keeps its higher `maxBullets()` cap ‚Äî so Rapid+Triple together is now the strongest combo (fires fast *and* wide, FLAG B-6-a), flagged for playtest rather than pre-emptively rebalanced. GDD ¬ß2.2 updated with the new cooldown values and the combo flag; Architecture Map constants row updated. Prior session: **v3.0 Phase 1 ‚Äî starfield legibility & parallax (B-3).** The starfield already existed (`drawStarfield`, `stars[]`, flat `STAR_DENSITY=40` at `#1a2a40`) ‚Äî this enhances it in place, no second system. (1) Each star now carries a per-star brightness `a` (`STAR_BRIGHT_MIN/MAX` = 0.35‚Äì1.0) drawn in a brighter cool blue (`rgba(120,160,210,a)`) so the field reads without competing with entities (Pillar 1). (2) `STAR_DENSITY` raised 40‚Üí80 (scales by world area, one knob). (3) Added **one** nearer parallax layer (`starsNear[]`, `STAR_NEAR_DENSITY=22`, brighter `rgba(160,195,235,a)`, `STAR_PARALLAX_FACTOR=0.5`) so the ship's motion produces visible relative drift. Per FLAG B-3-a, a ‚âÝ1√ó layer isn't world-fixed, so it can't reuse `shortDelta`/wrap math ‚Äî it's tiled in **screen space** instead (a 3√ó3 `VIEW_W√óVIEW_H` tile stamp keyed off `camera * STAR_PARALLAX_FACTOR`, culled to viewport), which sidesteps seam artifacts entirely. The original far layer is untouched structurally (still world-fixed, wrap-aware, 1.0√ó) and remains the depth reference. Five new constants (`STAR_PARALLAX_FACTOR`, `STAR_BRIGHT_MIN/MAX`, `STAR_NEAR_DENSITY`, `STAR_NEAR_BRIGHT_MIN/MAX`) join the retuned `STAR_DENSITY` in the v1.2 world block. Purely cosmetic ‚Äî zero gameplay effect, nothing in `update()` touched. Prior session: **added a dotted world-boundary line** ‚Äî a dim, dashed `WORLD_W√óWORLD_H` rectangle rendered at the wrap seam so the player can see the wrap-around coming and crossing it. `drawWorldBoundary()` (near `drawStarfield`) strokes the rect via `setLineDash([BOUNDARY_DASH, BOUNDARY_GAP])` + the existing `glowStroke` at `COLOR.dim` with low glow; it's the first thing drawn inside the camera transform (beneath every entity), positioned at the world-origin corner's **nearest wrapped image** relative to the camera (`wrapOffset` on both axes) so the seam shows whether the ship is near world x‚âà0 or x‚âàWORLD_W (y likewise) and stays continuous across the crossing. Purely cosmetic ‚Äî no collision, no gameplay effect. Four new tuning constants (`BOUNDARY_DASH/GAP/WIDTH/GLOW`) live in the v1.2 world block. This is an **interim** wrap-visibility aid; full off-screen threat awareness stays parked for v3.0. Prior session: **housekeeping ‚Äî archived the two spent v2.0 planning docs** (`PLANNED-FEATURES-v2.md` + `IMPLEMENTATION-PHASES.md`) into `archive/` after verifying every shipped v2.0 feature has its spec in GDD ¬ß2 (no doc-handoff gaps); no code change. Before that: implemented **F9 ‚Äî Achievements System**, the final v2.0 phase. Added an `Achievements` module holding two pools ‚Äî **15 weekly** (a calendar-deterministic 5-wide slice active each ISO week) and **12 lifetime** (cumulative across games) ‚Äî that **observes** stats the rest of the game already produces via one-liner hooks at each event's existing site (kills in `destroyDebris`/`destroyHunter`, deliveries in the dock-offload block, hits in `damageShip`, deflects at the four shield-absorb sites, powerups in `applyPowerup`, expiries in `Garbage.update`, perfect waves in the wave-clear block, best-wave in `nextWave`) ‚Äî **no new indirection layers, no restructured systems**. Per-game counters live in a flat `game.stats` bag (`resetGameStats()`, reset in `startGame`); lifetime counters + unlock sets persist to their **own** `localStorage` key (`afd_achievements_v1`, separate from settings), guarded + try/caught exactly like F8. Weekly rotation is pure math ‚Äî pool index `(isoYear*52 + isoWeek) % 15`, 5 consecutive entries wrapping the pool, from the real UTC date at launch ‚Äî so **every player worldwide sees the same 5 in the same calendar week**; a new week resets weekly unlocks while lifetime is always retained. An unlock pops a non-blocking gold **toast** (`AudioSys.achievement()` fanfare, aged out in the main loop by `updateToasts` so it animates in every state) and is browsable in a read-only **viewer at Pause ‚Üí Options ‚Üí Achievements** (`drawAchievements`: this week's 5 + the 12 lifetime, each with unlock status + `cur/goal` progress). `Achievements.evaluate()` runs once per frame (already-unlocked entries short-circuit) and again at game over (so end-of-game checks like Waste Not can fire). **v3.6 P3 (this session) ‚Äî powerup drops become three deterministic sources.** Read `PLANNED-FEATURES-v3.6.md` ¬ß5 + CONFLICT-3/CONFLICT-4 first, then grepped every call site before editing (`asteroids-deluxe.html`). Deleted `POWERUP_DROP_CHANCE` and both `maybeDropPowerup()` call sites (`destroyDebris`'s and `destroyHunter`'s small-tier branches) ‚Äî Debris now drops nothing, ever, and small-tier Hunter kills no longer drop either. Reworked `maybeDropPowerup` into an unconditional `dropPowerup(x, y, vx, vy)`: still rolls the same `POWERUP_DROP_WEIGHTS` table (untouched, `scoop` still absent from `POWERUP_DROP_TYPES` ‚Äî Constraint 2 verified unaffected), but the *chance gate is gone*; callers now decide **when**, this only decides **what**. Three call sites replace the old roll: (1) **every Saucer kill, large or small** ‚Äî extracted a new `destroySaucer(s)` flow function (shaped like `destroyDebris`/`destroyHunter`) as the choke point for the two previously copy-pasted saucer-kill sites (player-bullet branch and shield-body-contact branch), removing that duplication hazard; the drop inherits the saucer's `vx, vy` exactly, no scaling. (2) **every large Hunter core** (`h.size === 3` only, not its medium/small children) in `destroyHunter`'s split branch, also inheriting `h.vx, h.vy`. (3) **the recycle hub**, latched on `game.deliveryCount === 10` (one line above the existing `=== 12` Heavy Hauler latch, same "passes through exactly once per visit" idiom) ‚Äî emits one powerup from the dock's own position at a new `DOCK_POWERUP_SPEED` (120 px/s, PLAYTEST KNOB) in a random direction, plus a "SALVAGE BONUS" `FloatText` at the dock so the causality reads clearly. Also deleted the drag in `Powerup.update()` (`vx *= Math.pow(0.4, dt)`, CONFLICT-4) ‚Äî a drop now flies on its vector until collected or expired instead of settling to a stop in under a second; byte-identical for ambient Health, which still spawns at rest via the untouched `spawnHealthPowerup()`/`POWERUP_HEALTH_GAP` timer. This is a deliberate, flagged economy shift (CONFLICT-3): today's field supply becomes saucers (one at a time, 12‚Äì30s gaps) + large Hunters (one per 13-kill lineage) + the hub, instead of a per-small-kill roll ‚Äî early waves with few Hunters and sparse saucers could run drier than before; flagged for playtest, not blocked. Extended `scratchpad/test-v33-p3.js` (owns the drop economy: constants, the weighted roll, a full 13-kill Debris lineage drops zero, a full 13-kill Hunter lineage drops exactly one from the large core, both saucer-kill paths each drop exactly one on the saucer's own vector with matching score/achievement counters as a regression guard on the `destroySaucer` extraction, and the drag-removal speed-retention check) and `scratchpad/test-p6.js` (owns dock offload: the hub's per-visit latch ‚Äî a 9-canister visit emits none, a 10-canister visit emits exactly one from the dock's position at `DOCK_POWERUP_SPEED`, an 11th/12th canister in the same visit emits no more). Also had to fix three now-stale regression tests that referenced the removed `maybeDropPowerup`/`POWERUP_DROP_CHANCE` identifiers directly in their `new Function` return lists (a plain identifier there throws `ReferenceError` if undefined, unlike a normal object literal): `test-f6.js` section (G) ‚Äî which used to force-roll the old chance gate ‚Äî is trimmed to the one invariant that still holds (Health never in the drop pool) and now defers full drop-economy coverage to `test-v33-p3.js`; `test-v31-coalesce.js`'s scrap-born-lineage check updated its expected powerup count from 9 (one per small kill) to 1 (the large core only). Full regression re-run clean (22 files, all green) after fixing one real test bug of my own: the new dock-hub test initially forced the ship to sit exactly on the dock's own coordinates every frame, which (a) fought the tow-chain's real reaction physics when the chain had been built against a different ship position, occasionally yanking the ship back mid-test, and (b) meant POWERUP_RADIUS is pinned at LEVER_POWERUP_SIZE's disabled-lever 2x (30px, not the raw 15px constant), giving a 43px pickup radius that a same-tile ship instantly collects; fixed by building the chain against the ship's final resting spot and parking it just inside the `DOCK_RADIUS+10` near-dock cutoff but outside the 43px pickup circle.

**v2.0 (Phases 1‚Äì9), v3.0 (Phases 1‚Äì8), v3.1 (P1‚ÄìP3), and v3.2 (P1‚ÄìP3) are all shipped; v3.3 Phase 1 of 4 is now landed.** The **achievements overhaul (Part A) is complete** ‚Äî P7's tier infrastructure + converted lifetime set and P8's seven new tiered lifetime/event achievements + the "Flawless Run" weekly + the 16-pool rotation ‚Äî with its spec now fully in **GDD ¬ß2.17** (tier model + SUM/MAX note + the 16 weekly / 19 lifetime lists + `afd_achievements_v2`) + the Architecture Map Achievements/Constants rows; **Part A of `PLANNED-FEATURES-v3.md` is flipped to ‚úÖ SHIPPED**. - **Per-tier boundaries, all 7 new ladders** ‚Äî `threshold-1` stays on the prior tier and the exact threshold advances exactly one, for sharpshooter/freight_baron/zen_master/daredevil/wave_rider (SUM) + salvage_king/field_sweeper (MAX).
- **Event-cadence hooks driven through the REAL dock offload / game over** ‚Äî Freight Baron counts a ‚â•12 visit **exactly once** (not per canister past 12), a second visit ‚Üí 2, an 11-canister visit doesn't count; Zen Master counts a 5-streak haul **exactly once**, and a fresh 5-streak after a reset counts again ‚Üí 2; Daredevil + Wave Rider tally once at real `killShip` from a wave-6/no-Health/10-deflect game, and a Health-picked / under-10-deflect game tallies **neither**.
- **MAX-via-real-events** ‚Äî Field Sweeper tracks best Debris/game through 15 real `destroyDebris` kills; Salvage King tracks best delivered/game (15 in one visit, 20 across a run) through the real dock path.
- **Flawless Run** ‚Äî a damage-free **wave-7** clear does NOT arm it (floor is 8); a damage-free **wave-8** clear (driven through the real wave-clear loop) sets `flawlessLateWave` and unlocks the weekly.
- **Viewer** ‚Äî `drawAchievements` renders the widened 3-column mixed tiered/single-goal layout (19 lifetime across two columns) crash-free, both a mixed-tier state and an all-pre-bronze state.
- **Prior session (v3.0 P7):** drives the REAL `evaluate`/`deriveLifetime`/`nextWave`/`init`/`save` code (no reimplementation).
- **Config/tier structure** ‚Äî exactly **7 tiered** lifetime achievements (the P7 named set), every ladder is 6 strictly-ascending steps and carries **no** single-goal; `TIER_NAMES`/`TIER_COLOR` are length 6; `maxWaveNoPowerup` exists; `STORAGE_KEY === "afd_achievements_v2"`; The Long Haul is non-tiered goal-10 with a `12+` desc.
- **Per-tier boundaries (all 7 ladders)** ‚Äî for every threshold, `threshold-1` leaves you on the prior tier and the exact threshold advances **exactly one** tier (also exercises multi-tier catch-up in one pass). An explicit **cross-bronze-not-silver** fires exactly one Bronze toast; a **10,000-delivered jump crosses bronze+silver+gold in one pass** ‚Üí **three** ascending, tier-named toasts.
- **SUM vs MAX, through the real `nextWave`** ‚Äî `maxWaveNoPowerup` rises to 15 on a powerup-free `nextWave` (‚Üí No Powerups Needed Gold), then is **frozen at 5** when a powerup is picked before a deeper wave (only Silver); Master of the Field + Century Club coexist on `maxWave` (25 ‚Üí Master Gold + Century Club).
- **Viewer text** ‚Äî tiered status reads `"Gold ¬∑ 12,431 ‚Üí 25,000"`, `"Diamond ‚úì MAX"` at the ceiling, `"‚Äî ¬∑ 0 ‚Üí 1,000"` pre-bronze; non-tiered rows still read `cur/goal` and the play-time `1.0/10h`.
- **Persistence v2 + migration** ‚Äî a v2 save round-trips counters **and** per-id tier indices; a stale-low stored tier is **advanced** (never lowered) by `deriveLifetime`; a `_v1`-only save **migrates** (keeps raw counters, re-derives tiers ‚Äî 26k delivered ‚Üí Titanium, 60 Hunters ‚Üí Bronze ‚Äî ignores old flat unlock sets) and seeds **silently** (zero toasts); a corrupt v2 payload doesn't crash `init`.
- **Regression within F9** ‚Äî the ISO-week math + deterministic 15-pool rotation, weekly week-reset/lifetime-retained persistence, and every C1‚ÄìC6 real-gameplay unlock (debris/deliveries/close-shave/powerups/lineage/perfect-wave) + the toast lifecycle all stay green.

**Headless-verified prior session (v3.0 P6, `scratchpad/test-p6.js`, 37 assertions):** drives the REAL dock-offload path, `Ship.update`, and `updateChain` (no reimplementation).
- **Config** ‚Äî `CARGO_BASE`=12, `CARGO_CAP_MAX`=20, `CARGO_GROW_PER`=30 (positive), `CHAIN_ITER`‚â•3; retuned `CARGO_THRUST`=0.06 / `CARGO_MAXSPD`=0.03 / `CARGO_MASS`=0.07; the old `CHAIN_MAX` constant is gone from the source.
- **Cap growth is real** ‚Äî driving actual dock deliveries through `update()`: `cargoMax` starts at 12, stays 12 at 29 delivered, hits 13 at exactly 30, 14 at 60, 20 (ceiling) at 240, and **never exceeds** `CARGO_CAP_MAX` across 250 deliveries (exactly 8 increases, one per threshold); each bump pushes a "TOW +1" float; `startGame` resets it to 12.
- **Pickup gate + HUD read `cargoMax`** ‚Äî at `cargoMax`=12 a 13th field canister is refused; raising `cargoMax` to 16 lets the chain grow past 12; `draw()` is crash-free with a 20-node chain / cargoMax-20 HUD.
- **Physics retune, measured through the real `Ship.update`** ‚Äî a full chain at m=20 gives thrustMul ‚âà 0.4545 (45%) and top-speed ratio ‚âà 0.625 (63%), matching both the formula and the old full-12 feel; a base-12 chain is measurably lighter than the old-12 on both; Engine at 20 nodes ‚â° plain 10 nodes (FLAG B-8-a); the momentum-tug massFactor uses the 0.07 coeff (0.84 at m=12 uncapped, capped 1.4 at m=20), backed out from the real `updateChain` tug impulse.
- **Constraint stability at `CARGO_CAP_MAX` (20) nodes** ‚Äî 900 frames of hard thrust-flips across a wrap: no NaN, no node-velocity explosion, worst-case link stretch < one link length (‚âà4 px), no nodes lost/duplicated. (Iteration-count rationale reproduced in `scratchpad/diag-chain-iter.js`: 3‚Üí4‚Üí5 iters give 4.36‚Üí3.70‚Üí3.24 px worst stretch; 4 chosen.)

**Headless-verified prior session (v3.0 P5, `scratchpad/test-p5.js`, 57 assertions):** drives the REAL fire block, magnet/hook pass, menu state machine, and persistence (no reimplementation).
- **Config + defaults** ‚Äî both modes default `"time"`; `MENU_OPTIONS` has a `"Difficulty"` row sitting immediately before `"Back"`; `POWERUP_BUDGET` maps rapid/triple/magnet to `RAPID_SHOTS`/`TRIPLE_SHOTS`/`MAGNET_PIECES` (all positive).
- **Mode routing** ‚Äî `powerMode` sends rapid/triple to `shotPowerupMode`, magnet to `magnetMode`, and Engine to `"time"` **always** (even with count modes set ‚Äî Engine isn't configurable).
- **Default time = shipped behaviour, exactly** ‚Äî in time mode `applyPowerup` sets the timer (not the budget); firing does **not** touch `powerBudget`; rapid cadence still applies via the timer; a magnet hook spends **no** budget (and still hooks). Engine always uses the timer.
- **`"shots"` mode ends Rapid at EXACTLY `RAPID_SHOTS` pulls** ‚Äî one pull spends one; still active with 1 left; inactive the pull that hits 0; the last rapid pull still fired at `RAPID_FIRE_COOLDOWN` and the first post-expiry pull returns to `FIRE_COOLDOWN`.
- **A Triple 3-fan is ONE pull** ‚Äî one pull fires 3 bullets and spends exactly one `triple` shot.
- **Rapid + Triple budgets are independent** ‚Äî driving `TRIPLE_SHOTS` pulls exhausts Triple while Rapid is left at exactly `RAPID_SHOTS ‚àí TRIPLE_SHOTS` and still active; with Triple gone a pull fires a single bullet at rapid cadence; Rapid then ends on its own budget.
- **`"pieces"` mode ends Magnet at EXACTLY `MAGNET_PIECES` hooks** ‚Äî one hooked canister spends exactly one piece (B-5-a: a draw-then-hook doesn't double-spend); active with 1 left; inactive at 0; no further spend once inactive.
- **Same-type refresh restores the budget to full, never stacks** ‚Äî a partially-spent Rapid/Magnet budget returns to full on re-pickup; a second refresh does not exceed full.
- **Difficulty screen** ‚Äî reachable Options ‚Üí Difficulty; ‚óÑ/‚ñ∫ on each row selects time/count; down walks shot ‚Üí magnet ‚Üí Back; Back (and the `back` action) return to Options with the cursor on Difficulty; menu toggles persist and reload; a direct `saveSettings`/`loadSettings` round-trips; an **old save missing the mode keys** loads clean (defaults kept); a **bogus** mode value is ignored while a valid sibling still loads.
- **Draw crash-free** ‚Äî the Difficulty screen (both toggle states), the Options screen with the new row, and the **count-mode HUD** (active Rapid/Triple/Magnet numeric bars + Engine timed bar) all render without throwing.

- **Controller Start = session toggle** ‚Äî Start on title ‚Üí starts a game; Start while playing ‚Üí opens the pause root (`MENU_ROOT_PLAY`); Start while paused ‚Üí dismisses & resumes.

- **ESC pauses outside a menu, backs inside** ‚Äî ESC while playing opens the pause root; ESC in Options backs to root, ESC at root resumes; ESC on the title with no menu is inert (O/B are the openers).
- **A/Enter still start a game** from title/gameover.
- **FLAG P4-b holds three ways** ‚Äî Enter inside the system menu navigates and never restarts; a same-frame pad **B+A** opens the menu without also starting (else-if guard); A while the system menu is open confirms in-menu, no start.
- **No leak** ‚Äî nav keys pressed while a menu is open are never written to `keys{}`, no menu keypress starts a game, and `update()` stays frozen while paused (a held gameplay key can't rotate the ship).
- **Achievements dual-entry backs correctly** ‚Äî reached from the system root it backs to root (cursor on Achievements, `achReturn="root"`); reached via Options it backs to Options (`achReturn="options"`).

As flagged, the fix belonged to a chain/powerup-owning session (this one): **`test-f3`'s `resetShip` now zeroes `game.powerFx`**, so every (D) scenario starts powerup-free. Confirmed **10/10 green** after the fix (was ~4/6 failing before). Not a code change to the game ‚Äî a test-harness fix only.

## Known issues

- **Real-`localStorage` persistence is unverified across the board (v1.9 + v2.0 + v3.0 P7/P8).** Both the settings key (`afd_settings_v1`) and the achievements key (**`afd_achievements_v2`** ‚Äî bumped in P7 from `_v1`, **unchanged in P8** since the seven new counters ride the existing known-key load/save) round-trip headlessly against a stub, but real cross-session persistence can only be confirmed in a browser running the file locally (the claude.ai artifact sandbox has no `localStorage`). All access is `typeof`-guarded + try/caught, so the sandbox worst case is "progress just doesn't persist," never a crash. **The P7 `_v1‚Üí_v2` migration (keep counters, re-derive tier badges, drop old unlock sets ‚Äî FLAG A-2-a) is best-effort and browser-unverified: a returning v2.1 player's lifetime counters should survive and tiers recompute, but their current-week weekly unlocks may reset once.** **Top persistence playtest item.**
- **A few starter achievements are intentionally hard or degenerate (v2.0), by design of the starter pool ‚Äî not bugs.** *Waste Not* ("zero canisters expired in a game") is near-impossible to earn legitimately (a lineage sheds 39‚Äì66 canisters and the chain caps at 12), yet is trivially satisfiable by dying before anything decays ‚Äî it's implemented literally per F9's list. Curating/balancing the pools (retiring degenerate ones, tuning thresholds) is a **post-playtest pass**, deliberately not done this phase.
- **Weekly achievements reset each calendar week (v2.0), by design.** Unlocking a weekly one records it only for the current ISO week; when the week rolls over the 5 change and weekly-unlock progress starts fresh (lifetime never resets). This is the intended "weekly challenge" model ‚Äî flagged so a mid-week reset (which won't happen ‚Äî the week only changes on Monday UTC) isn't mistaken for data loss.
- ~~**Achievements viewer is reachable only from Pause ‚Üí Options (v2.0).**~~ **RESOLVED in v3.0 P4.** The Options/Achievements system menu now opens directly from the title/gameover screen (keyboard "O", controller B); its root offers Achievements as a first-class entry. The old "start a game to browse achievements" limitation (and the parallel F8 "menu reachable only via pause" note) is closed.
- **Gamepad rebind drops that action's analog axis (v1.9), by design.** Capturing reads a button, not a stick direction; Return to Defaults restores the axis.
- **Audio unlock on a controller-only start is browser-dependent (v1.8).** Best-effort `AudioSys.init()`/`resume()` on Start/A, but the Web Audio autoplay policy generally wants a keyboard/pointer gesture ‚Äî a controller-only player may hear nothing (incl. the new achievement fanfare + menu blips) until one keyboard press.
- **Soft weapon cap (v1.7), by design:** a Triple volley can transiently exceed the 12-bullet cap by up to 2.
- **Performance watch (v1.4/v1.6; sharper as of v3.2 P3):** heavy `shadowBlur`; garbage-dense late waves are the stress case (a cleared *timer-spawned* Hunter lineage sheds 66 canisters; a scrap-born one sheds 0). **v3.2 P3 removed the decay timer that used to bound coexistence ‚Äî garbage is permanent now**, so late waves can carry more standing salvage; render is viewport-culled (draw cost is bounded), and the O(n¬≤) `coalesceGarbage` pass is the watch item (FLAG D-2). Levers: a global glow toggle, then the drop-volume constants (`DEBRIS_GARBAGE`/`HUNTER_SMALL_GARBAGE`), then (only if a stress test shows it) a spatial hash for coalescence. The v2.0 achievement layer adds negligible per-frame cost (‚âà17 simple `cur()` compares, already-unlocked short-circuit).

## Balance notes

- **Powerup drop economy (v3.6 P3) ‚Äî one new first-pass playtest knob, browser feel unverified.** `DOCK_POWERUP_SPEED` (120 px/s) is the only new constant; the hub launches its per-visit drop on this speed in a random direction from the dock's own position. The bigger open question is the economy shift itself (CONFLICT-3, flagged not blocked): Debris now drops nothing at all (was the *only* small-tier roll site along with small Hunters), so field supply is now saucers (12‚Äì30s gaps) + one per full large-Hunter lineage + one per 10-canister dock visit ‚Äî early waves with few Hunters and sparse saucers could run drier than the old per-kill roll. If it plays too dry, the dial to reach for first is the dock latch threshold (currently every 10th canister, one line above the existing `=== 12` Heavy Hauler latch) ‚Äî lowering it increases hub frequency without touching the two kill-based sources.
- **Magnet buff (v3.6 P2a) ‚Äî three first-pass playtest knobs, browser feel unverified.** `MAGNET_FALLOFF_POW` (2‚Üí1, linear), `MAGNET_PULL_MIN` (60‚Üí150), `MAGNET_DAMP` (0.06‚Üí0.35) all live in the constants block with a derived-`v_terminal` comment above the pull block explaining why `MAGNET_DAMP` (not `MAGNET_PULL`) is the lever that matters. `MAGNET_DAMP` is explicitly the riskiest of the three per spec ‚Äî if pieces overshoot/orbit the ship instead of landing, pull it back toward 0.06 before touching the other two. `MAGNET_RANGE` (380) and `MAGNET_PULL` (520) are untouched.
- **Large-Hunter last-stand pursuit (v3.6 P2b) ‚Äî two first-pass playtest knobs, browser feel unverified.** `HUNTER_LAST_STAND_SPEED` (50 px/s) and `HUNTER_LAST_STAND_TURN` (0.5 rad/s), both new constants near the Hunter block. Deliberately slow/under-specified per spec ‚Äî the open question is pure feel: does the pursuit read clearly as "the wave is ending" without a silhouette change (the core keeps its tumbling diamond throughout ‚Äî FLAG-G), and does it stay a "search-ender" rather than a second homing tier at these speeds.
- **World shrink (v3.1 P1) ‚Äî a first-pass size, browser feel unverified.** `WORLD_W/H` 3840√ó2160‚Üí2560√ó1440 (~44% of the old area) is meant to cut the dead-space feel of the old 9√ó world; the ship-relative spawn/dock rings were clamped to match so nothing is unreachable. Open question is purely feel: does the smaller world read as "denser, more populated" without feeling cramped or making the wrap seam come around too often during normal play? `WORLD_W/H` is the single knob if it needs another pass (re-derive the spawn-ring clamp and re-soften if changed again ‚Äî see the note in "Notes for a future session").

- **Tow-cap progression + chain retune (v3.0 P6) ‚Äî first-pass numbers, browser feel unverified.** `CARGO_BASE` (12), `CARGO_CAP_MAX` (20), `CARGO_GROW_PER` (30 delivered per +1) and the retuned `CARGO_THRUST` (0.06) / `CARGO_MAXSPD` (0.03) / `CARGO_MASS` (0.07) / `CHAIN_ITER` (4) are all single-knob tunables in the salvage/chain block. The retune math is exact (full 20-chain reproduces the old full-12 ratios), and stability is headless-solid, but three things are **feel/perf, browser-only:** (1) does a full max chain feel *heavy but drivable* (not broken) ‚Äî and does the now-lighter base-12 chain feel *too* light? (2) does the cap-growth cadence feel *earned* ‚Äî is +1 per 30 delivered (‚âà240 delivered to reach 20, roughly 8‚Äì16 waves of active hauling) too slow or about right? (3) any whip/perf issues (`shadowBlur`, FLAG B-8-c) in dense late waves at 20 nodes? `CARGO_GROW_PER` is the cadence lever; the three coefficients are the feel levers; a global glow toggle is the perf lever (decay is gone as of v3.2 P3). See the new playtest ask below.
- **Powerup expiry count budgets (v3.0 P5) ‚Äî first-pass numbers, no playtest feedback yet, and OFF by default.** `RAPID_SHOTS` (40), `TRIPLE_SHOTS` (30), `MAGNET_PIECES` (20) only bite when the player opts into `"shots"`/`"pieces"` on the Difficulty screen; the default `"time"` path is untouched (still `POWERUP_DURATION` = 15 s). These three are single-knob tunables in the Powerups block. Open questions are all *feel*, browser-only: do 40 rapid / 30 triple pulls and 20 magnet hooks feel like a fair "use it or lose it" trade vs. the 15 s clock; is the Rapid+Triple *independent* decrement legible (Triple running out mid-fight while Rapid keeps single shots going); and is the count HUD (numeric label beside the bar) readable at a glance. Note the cross-mode interaction with the P2 fire-rate work: rapid cadence keys off `powerActive("rapid")`, so in shots mode the fast cadence lasts exactly `RAPID_SHOTS` pulls.
- **TARGETS HUD (v3.0 P3) ‚Äî no balance knobs, a pure readout.** No new tuning constants; it's two existing array lengths (`game.debris.length + game.hunters.length`) read into the HUD. The one open question is presentational, not numeric ‚Äî whether the single `TARGETS n` count (chosen) reads clearly when it jumps up on a Hunter arrival, vs. the two-part `DEBRIS n ¬∑ HUNTERS m` fallback named in `PLANNED-FEATURES-v3.md` B-7 (see playtest ask below).
- **Fire-rate rebalance (v3.0 P2) ‚Äî first-pass numbers, no playtest feedback yet.** `FIRE_COOLDOWN` 0.16‚Üí0.20 (base gun ~6.25‚Üí5 shots/sec) and new `RAPID_FIRE_COOLDOWN` 0.09 (~11 shots/sec) are single-knob tunables in the weapons block. **Rapid+Triple is now a strictly stronger combo than either alone** (fast cadence + wide spread, FLAG B-6-a) ‚Äî previously Rapid only raised the cap, so this is a real balance shift, not just a bug fix. Wants a playtest read on whether the slower base feels sluggish and whether Rapid+Triple needs a cap/cooldown interaction to stay in check.
- **Starfield (v3.0 P1) ‚Äî five first-pass tunables, no playtest feedback yet.** `STAR_DENSITY` (40‚Üí80), `STAR_PARALLAX_FACTOR` (0.5), `STAR_BRIGHT_MIN/MAX` (0.35‚Äì1.0), `STAR_NEAR_DENSITY` (22), `STAR_NEAR_BRIGHT_MIN/MAX` (0.55‚Äì1.0) are all single-knob tunables in the v1.2 world block. Density/brightness/parallax strength all want a playtest read (see Playtest asks below) before calling this feature done.
- **New achievements (v3.0 P8) ‚Äî 8 first-pass ladders/floors + a viewer relayout, all browser-unverified.** The seven new tiered ladders (Sharpshooter 100‚Üí**7,500**, Freight Baron/Zen Master 1‚Üí1,000, Daredevil/Wave Rider 1‚Üí**300**, Salvage King 10‚Üí200, Field Sweeper 15‚Üí400) and the Flawless Run floor (`game.wave >= 8`) are single-line tunables; the FLAG-A-8-a diamond (7,500) and FLAG-A-12-a softenings (300) are the deliberate deviations from Paul's proposed numbers. Open questions are all feel (see Playtest asks 7a‚Äì7c): are the new goals earnable-but-meaningful, is wave 8 the right Flawless floor, do the per-EVENT counters climb at a satisfying rate. Salvage King's per-game-best ladder tops at 200 ‚Äî re-check against the raised tow cap (FLAG A-9-a: cap ceiling is 20, so no nudge deemed needed, but browser-confirm). The viewer relayout (widened 1200√ó660 3-column) is a **look-call I picked, not spec'd** ‚Äî ask 7d + the "surfaced" note in Next up.
- **Tiered achievements (v3.0 P7) ‚Äî the tier badge palette + the seven ladders are first-pass, all browser-unverified.** `TIER_COLOR[]` (bronze‚Üídiamond) is a pure look-call tunable ‚Äî the only real question is whether the six badge tints **read as ranks and never as hazard/enemy tells** (FLAG A-1-a), especially the pale top three (gold/titanium/platinum/diamond) against a busy field. The seven ladders come straight from the ¬ßA-3 table (kept as-proposed) ‚Äî they want a read on whether the low tiers land early enough to feel rewarding and the diamond ceilings (esp. **No Powerups Needed** wave-29, FLAG A-6-a) read as an aspirational flex rather than a typo. Retuning a ladder = editing its `tiers:[‚Ä¶]` array; recolouring = editing `TIER_COLOR[]`. **One UX feel-question for the browser:** does a big lifetime jump popping **several toasts at once** (ascending, one per crossed tier) feel *good* (a satisfying cascade) or *spammy*? If spammy, the fix is to collapse a multi-crossing into a single "reached Gold" toast ‚Äî noted, not done.
- **Achievements (v2.0) ‚Äî thresholds are first-pass, no balance knobs beyond the four `ACH_*` constants.** `ACH_TOAST_TIME` (4.5 s), `ACH_WEEKLY_SHOWN` (5), `ACH_LINEAGE_FULL` (13 = a full Hunter lineage), `ACH_SAVE_EVERY` (30 s periodic save). The remaining single-goal numbers came straight from F9's starter pools ‚Äî they want a playtest read on whether they're *earnable but meaningful* (see playtest asks). Adding/retiring achievements is just editing the `WEEKLY`/`LIFETIME` arrays; a longer weekly rotation before repeats is "add more weekly ideas," not a structural change.
- **Carried forward, unchanged:** menu `VOL_STEP` (0.1) and `GP_DEADZONE` (0.25) (v1.9/v1.8); `POWERUP_HEALTH_GAP` ([18,26]), `POWERUP_DURATION` (15), weapon caps (Rapid 8 / Triple 12), `MAGNET_*`, `ENGINE_MASS_MULT` (0.5) (v1.7 ‚Äî `POWERUP_DROP_CHANCE` removed in v3.6 P3, see Balance notes below); the Hunter tables + `HUNTER_FLOOR_FRAC` (0.58) + shared `RAMP_WAVES` (8) (v1.6/v1.5); wave spawn `min(3+wave, 9)` (v1.4). *(`GARBAGE_DECAY`/`GARBAGE_SEVER_DECAY` removed in v3.2 P3 ‚Äî garbage is permanent.)*
- **Still open: the joint F3+F10 Debris-density retune.** The one remaining v2.0 tuning lever ‚Äî with every combat/utility/UI system now in, judge the *combined* early-game field feel in a browser, then lean on coalescence (`GARBAGE_MAGNET_RANGE`/`GARBAGE_COALESCE_DELAY`) and the drop-volume constants for density (decay is gone as of v3.2 P3). A post-playtest pass, not a number to guess.
