**v3.2 Phase 3 of N (salvage permanent + economy closed) is landed this session.** Active plan docs: `PLANNED-FEATURES-v3.2.md` / `IMPLEMENTATION-PHASES-v3.2.md`. **Next up:** whatever Phase 4+ scopes (v3.2 is "Phase 3 of N"). Notes carried forward for a future session:
- **Garbage is permanent now (v3.2 P3) ‚Äî there is no decay.** Never re-introduce a decay timer as a density lever (GDD ¬ß2.10.1 rewrote and explains why). A canister leaves the field only by being **recycled** or **coalescing into a Hunter**. Density levers are `GARBAGE_MAGNET_RANGE` / `GARBAGE_COALESCE_DELAY` / `HUNTER_COALESCE_COUNT` (coalescence throughput) and the drop-volume constants (`DEBRIS_GARBAGE`/`HUNTER_GARBAGE`/`HUNTER_SMALL_GARBAGE`, held in reserve).
- **A coalescence-born Hunter (`bornOfScrap`) drops NO garbage ‚Äî do not "fix" this.** The flag is set at the transform site in `coalesceGarbage` and propagated to split children in `destroyHunter`; the emission skip is the FORK-B/B1 sink that keeps the economy closed (12 in, 0 out). Timer-spawned Hunters keep `bornOfScrap = false` and drop the full 66. If you add a new Hunter spawn path, decide its `bornOfScrap` explicitly.
- **`GARBAGE_MAGNET_RANGE` (260) is the number most likely to be wrong (FLAG D-1)** ‚Äî flagged in-code. If the field silts up with inert junk (pieces that never clump and never get collected), raise it; if clumps form too aggressively, lower it. `GARBAGE_COALESCE_DELAY` (6.0 s) is the companion knob (how long a fresh burst drifts before it can re-clump).
- **`coalesceGarbage` is still O(n¬≤)** with permanent garbage ‚Äî no spatial hash added this phase (FLAG D-2, deliberately out of scope). Render is viewport-culled so free-canister count doesn't drive draw cost. If a late-wave stress test shows the pair-test cost, a spatial hash is the follow-up.
- **Waste Not now keys on `game.stats.hunterCoalesced === 0`** (not the removed `garbageDecayed`). The id + pool slot were kept, so the weekly-rotation math and `test-f9` slices are unchanged ‚Äî don't recompute them.

**v3.0 (all 8 phases) is fully shipped and closed out ‚Äî "Phase 9" never existed.** v2.0 and v3.0 are both archived under `archive/` (`archive/PLANNED-FEATURES-v2.md`/`archive/IMPLEMENTATION-PHASES-v2.md`, `archive/PLANNED-FEATURES-v3.md`/`archive/IMPLEMENTATION-PHASES-v3.md`, `archive/README.md`) ‚Äî current design authority is `orbital-overhaul-GDD.md` ¬ß2 + active `PLANNED-FEATURES-v3.1.md`/`IMPLEMENTATION-PHASES.md` at the repo root; build reality is this file. **v3.1 Phase 1 of N (world shrink + spawn-ring clamp) is landed this session; Phase 2 (fix the `+120` wrap-jump discontinuity) is next.** Candidate directions from here:
- **Continue the v3.1 phase order** ‚Äî **Phase 2 next** (see `IMPLEMENTATION-PHASES.md` for its scope: the `updateChain` wrap jumps by `WORLD_W/H + 120` instead of exactly `WORLD_W/H`, a pre-existing ~120px seam discontinuity ‚Äî not touched this phase, flagged in the P1 prompt as explicitly out of scope).
- **‚öÝ SURFACED THIS SESSION (a design call the P8 plan didn't scope ‚Äî needs Paul's read):** growing LIFETIME 12‚Üí19 overflowed the achievements viewer's single lifetime column. Implemented a reasonable fit ‚Äî widened the panel to **1200√ó660** and split lifetime across **two columns** (three total: weekly | lifetime | lifetime-cont.). It's crash-tested and in-idiom, but the **layout/column-split/panel-width is a look-call I picked, not a spec'd one** ‚Äî confirm it reads well in a browser (or say if you'd prefer a scroll, curated display, or different split). All layout numbers are one-line tunables in `drawAchievements`.
- **Playtest the P8 achievements** (new asks below): whether the new goals feel earnable-but-meaningful, whether Flawless Run @ wave 8 is the right floor, and whether the per-event counters (Freight Baron / Zen Master) climb at a satisfying rate. Plus the P7 tier badges/colours + toast cascade and the longer-standing full v2.0 consolidated asks ‚Äî especially real `localStorage` persistence (now the `_v1‚Üí_v2` migration too, still browser-unverified) and achievement threshold feedback.
- **The joint F3+F10 Debris-density retune** (the last v2.0 balance lever ‚Äî see Balance notes).

Notes for a future session:
- **The tow cap is runtime now (v3.0 P6), not a constant.** Read `game.cargoMax` (never a fixed 12) at any pickup-cap or HUD site; it grows 12‚Üí20 per `CARGO_GROW_PER` deliveries and resets in `startGame`. `CHAIN_MAX` no longer exists. The chain's stability envelope is revalidated at **20 nodes / `CHAIN_ITER` (4) iters** (GDD ¬ß3.4) ‚Äî if you ever lengthen the chain or link again, re-soften `CARGO_THRUST`/`CARGO_MAXSPD`/`CARGO_MASS` *together* (so a full chain at the new ceiling ‚âà old full-12 feel) and re-run the `test-p6` (E) stress, don't just bump the number. **Achievements must not key "full chain" on `cargoMax`** ‚Äî use a fixed ‚â•12 (FLAG B-8-b).
- **The two persistence keys are independent by design** ‚Äî `afd_settings_v1` (F8, now also the P5 difficulty modes) and **`afd_achievements_v2`** (F9, bumped in P7). Keep them separate. The P5 modes are **additive fields** on `afd_settings_v1` (no schema bump) ‚Äî always tolerate a missing/unknown value on load.
- **Achievements persistence is now `afd_achievements_v2` (v3.0 P7), shape `{lifetime, lifetimeTiers{id:idx}, lifetimeUnlocked[non-tiered], weekly{key,unlocked[]}}`.** Tiered lifetime state lives in `lifetimeTiers` (highest tier idx per id), non-tiered lifetime unlocks in `lifetimeUnlocked`. `init()` reads `_v2`; absent it, it migrates the old `_v1` **counters** only (tiers/unlocks re-derive) then ignores `_v1`. **`deriveLifetime()` runs after every load** to seed tiers/unlocks from counters *silently* (no toast) ‚Äî so anything that mutates a lifetime counter outside the normal hooks must let evaluate() catch up, and any NEW tiered achievement added later auto-back-fills its badge on next load without re-toasting. **A tiered entry has `tiers:[‚Ä¶]` and NO `goal`; a MAX-counter one updates via `Math.max` at its event (never `+=`).** The **four** MAX counters (v3.0 P8) are `maxWave`, `maxWaveNoPowerup`, `bestDeliveredGame`, `bestDebrisGame`. **P8 also proved the auto-back-fill claim:** its seven new tiered achievements added no persistence code ‚Äî the new counters ride the existing `loadCounters` known-key loop + `save` spread, and `deriveLifetime()` seeds their badges silently on load.
- **Powerup expiry is mode-aware now (v3.0 P5).** Route every "is effect X active?" read through **`powerActive(type)`** (never `game.powerFx.X > 0` directly) so time/count modes stay consistent ‚Äî the fire block, `maxBullets`, `chainMass`, the Magnet pull, and the HUD all do. Count budgets live in `game.powerBudget`; the two mode settings live on the module-level persisted `settings` object. **Engine is intentionally always time-based** (not in `powerBudget`, not on the Difficulty screen). Known edge: flipping a mode mid-effect can end that effect (it starts reading the other, zeroed counter) ‚Äî acceptable ("you changed the rules"). If B-4-c grows the Difficulty screen, add a `DIFFICULTY_ROWS` entry + a `menuDifficulty` switch case + a `drawDifficulty` row.
- **Achievements observe, never drive.** New achievements = add a `{id, pool, name, desc, goal|tiers, cur, text?}` entry to `WEEKLY`/`LIFETIME` and, if a new stat is needed, add the counter to the right home ‚Äî a **per-game** flag/count goes in `resetGameStats()` (read via `s.` in a weekly `cur`), a **lifetime** counter goes in `Achievements.lifetime` (read via `l.`) ‚Äî plus **one hook at the event's existing site**. Don't route gameplay through the module. **P8 patterns worth reusing:** a **per-EVENT latch** = increment at the moment a monotonic per-game counter passes the threshold exactly (`deliveryCount === 12`, `pacifistStreak === 5`) so it fires once per event, not per tick past it; a **once-per-game** lifetime tally = increment at `killShip` from the final per-game state (before the game-over `evaluate()`); a **MAX personal-best** = `Math.max(l.best, s.perGameCount)` at the per-game counter's own event site.
- ~~**The menu is still reachable only via pause.**~~ **Done in v3.0 P4** ‚Äî the title/gameover system menu (keyboard "O", controller B) delivers the options + achievements title-screen entry point.
- **The corrected P4 control scheme supersedes the planned B-1-a mapping (Start‚Üímenu).** If revisiting the menu/input design, note that Start is now the session toggle and B/"O" are the menu openers ‚Äî don't reintroduce Start‚Üímenu. FLAG P4-a resolved as "retire P"; FLAG P4-b guaranteed by the gamepad else-if chain + keyboard menu-open early return.
- **`WORLD_W`/`WORLD_H` and the spawn/dock ring maxes are coupled (v3.1 P1) ‚Äî never change one without the other.** The binding limit is `min(WORLD_W, WORLD_H)/2 ‚àí 60`; `SPAWN_MAX_DIST`/`DOCK_MAX_DIST` must stay under it or a ring can wrap around and place a spawn on the far side of the ship. If the world size changes again, recompute the limit and re-clamp both `_MAX_DIST` constants (mins are independent of world size and don't need to move). `STAR_DENSITY` never needs to change for a world-size edit ‚Äî `STAR_COUNT` is already area-derived.

## Playtest asks (Paul ‚Äî can't be checked headlessly)

**VoiceSys / Dan (CS010 P9) ‚Äî NEW this session (all the routing/latch/cooldown logic is headless-solid; everything here is feel/mix and needs a real browser + audio):**
13a. **Does Dan cut through the mix?** With SFX + music playing, is the Voice Volume default (1.0) balanced against them, or does he get buried / dominate? The Voice slider (Options ‚Üí Sound / Music ‚Üí Voice Volume) is the per-player lever; the in-mix default is a look-call.
13b. **Is the 1.2 s `VOICE_COOLDOWN` right?** Play a busy stretch ‚Äî do the lines feel like an occasional bark (good) or does Dan chatter over himself / go too quiet? And does the **priority** read right: a hull-critical line should clearly interrupt a lower one, and you should NEVER hear Dan narrate an event that finished seconds ago (superseded lines drop, by design).
13c. **Do the trigger anchors feel right in play?** Especially: hull-relief landing on the way back up (does it feel like relief, alongside P3's ring-exhale?); the dock tiers reading as a fair size-up of the haul; "Truck is full, let's go." landing exactly when the chain fills (which moves as `cargoMax` grows 12‚Üí24).
13d. **The unpause case (the whole reason this phase was careful):** drop to low HP, pause, wait, resume ‚Äî Dan should **NOT** re-say "Hull integrity is critical." (the siren tone restarting is correct; the *voice* must not). Confirm in a browser.
13e. **Sign-off/character/captions** ‚Äî see the four carried items under "Next up" (was the FLAG-11a sign-off real; radio-Dan vs clean synth; any uncommitted ‚úé phoneme fixes to re-port; captions yes/no).

**High Scores table size (CS010 P5) ‚Äî NEW this session:**
12a. **Is 1.8√ó the right scale on the browsable High Scores screen** (Options ‚Üí High Scores)? The panel grew to 1000√ó560 to fit it with air ‚Äî check it doesn't feel oversized/cramped in a real browser.
12b. **Now that the browsable table is bigger, does the gameover table (left at 1.0√ó, unchanged) read small by comparison?** If so, the fix is re-flowing the gameover screen (moving "PRESS ENTER TO PLAY AGAIN"/the O-hint) to afford a bigger table there too ‚Äî a separate, un-scoped job, not built this phase.

**Consolidated across Phases 1‚Äì9 (v3.0) + v3.1 + v3.2 ‚Äî everything below needs a real browser (some need a controller).** Ordered roughly newest-first.

**Powerup drop economy (v3.6 P3) ‚Äî NEW this session (the mechanics/counters/tests are headless-solid; everything here is feel/economy):**
11a. **Does the field feel too dry in early waves now that Debris drops nothing?** (CONFLICT-3, flagged not blocked.) Supply is now saucers (12‚Äì30s gaps) + one per full large-Hunter lineage + one per 10-canister dock visit ‚Äî play a few early waves and see if powerups feel rare enough to be frustrating rather than earned.
11b. **Does the recycle hub's "SALVAGE BONUS" drop read clearly as caused by the delivery**, or does it get lost against the field? It launches from the dock's position at `DOCK_POWERUP_SPEED` (120 px/s) in a random direction.
11c. **Do the saucer and large-Hunter drops feel like fair, noticeable rewards** for a UFO kill or clearing a whole Hunter lineage, now that they always drop instead of never (saucers) or only sometimes (Hunters)?
11d. **With drag removed, does a drop's straight-line flight ever carry it somewhere unreachable** (off toward empty space, out past the play area) before its 26s decay, versus the old settle-to-a-stop behavior?

**Magnet buff + large-Hunter last-stand pursuit (v3.6 P2) ‚Äî physics/pursuit logic is headless-solid; everything here is feel:**
10a. **Does the Magnet finally feel strong across the whole range**, not just near the ship? Fly a piece in from ~350px and see if the mid-field pull now reads as a real attraction rather than a nudge.
10b. **Does `MAGNET_DAMP` 0.35 make pieces overshoot and orbit the ship instead of landing?** This was the spec's own flagged risk for the biggest lever ‚Äî if pieces jitter/circle instead of gliding in and hooking, `MAGNET_DAMP` is the knob to pull back first (toward 0.06), not `MAGNET_PULL`.
10c. **Is a last-stand large core's slow pursuit legible** with no silhouette change (it keeps its tumbling diamond the whole time ‚Äî the pursuit itself is the only tell, FLAG-G)? If players don't notice, the cheap fix named in spec is heading-locking the tumble, not a new shape.
10d. **Does the last-stand core read as "the wave is ending," not as a second homing tier?** `HUNTER_LAST_STAND_SPEED` (50 px/s) is deliberately below even a wave-1 medium homer ‚Äî confirm it still feels distinctly slower/searchier, not like another threat closing in.

**Salvage permanent + economy closed (v3.2 P3) ‚Äî NEW this session (all mechanics/counters/tests are headless-solid; everything here is feel/perf/legibility):**
9a. **`GARBAGE_COALESCE_DELAY` (6.0 s):** do same-explosion siblings visibly drift apart and *later* find strangers ‚Äî or do they still snap together, or never clump at all?
9b. **`GARBAGE_MAGNET_RANGE` (260) ‚Äî the number most likely to be wrong (FLAG D-1):** does the field silt up with inert junk that never clumps and never gets collected? Too low ‚Üí junk accumulates; too high ‚Üí clumps form too aggressively.
9c. **Does the shatter loop actually fire?** Do you find yourself *hunting* clumps to break them for a near-full cargo run, or ignoring them until they Hunter?
9d. **Does a mass-11 clump read as heavy** (momentum-conserving merge + mass-weighted pull), or just as slow and boring?
9e. **Is the cluster silhouette legible** at speed against a busy field, and does it read as *garbage* rather than *enemy*?
9f. **Late-wave perf** with permanent garbage ‚Äî frame time at wave 10+, given the O(n¬≤) coalescence pass (FLAG D-2, no spatial hash yet).
9g. **Does B1 make letting a clump transform feel like a real choice** (a scrap-born lineage is pure score, no cleanup bill), or is shooting the clump always strictly correct?

**World shrink (v3.1 P1) ‚Äî NEW this session:**
8a. **Does the smaller 2560√ó1440 world feel right?** Fly around ‚Äî does it read as a denser, more populated field than before (less "empty space between spawns"), or does it now feel cramped / does the wrap seam come around distractingly often during normal play? `WORLD_W`/`WORLD_H` is the single knob (coupled to the spawn-ring clamp ‚Äî see "Notes for a future session" if it needs another pass).
8b. **Do spawn/dock placements ever feel too close or too far now?** The rings were proportionally the same but clamped down (`SPAWN_MAX_DIST` 1100‚Üí640, `DOCK_MAX_DIST` 900‚Üí620) ‚Äî confirm a fresh wave and a relocated dock both still feel reachable-but-not-trivial to reach.

**New tiered/event/weekly achievements (v3.0 P8) ‚Äî NEW this session (all the counter/latch/rotation/test logic is headless-solid; everything here is feel/look):**
7a. **Do the new goals feel earnable-but-meaningful?** Play through and watch the seven new tiered rows in Pause ‚Üí Options ‚Üí Achievements. Do the low tiers land early enough to feel rewarding, and do the ceilings read as aspirational (esp. Sharpshooter's 7,500 small-saucer diamond, and Salvage King/Field Sweeper's per-game bests)? Ladders are one-line `tiers:[‚Ä¶]` tunables.
7b. **Is Flawless Run @ wave 8 the right floor?** A damage-free clear of wave 8+ ‚Äî too hard (never happens in a normal run), too easy, or a good "weekly-worthy" feat distinct from No Scratches (wave 3)? The floor is the literal `game.wave >= 8` in the wave-clear block.
7c. **Do the per-EVENT counters (Freight Baron / Zen Master) climb at a satisfying rate?** Freight Baron ticks once per ‚â•12-canister dock visit; Zen Master once per 5-in-a-row no-fire haul. Over a session, do those accumulate at a rate that makes the 1/10/50/150/400/1000 ladder feel reachable-but-long, or too slow/fast? (Daredevil/Wave Rider are once-per-game by nature, hence their softened 1/5/20/50/125/300.)
7d. **Does the widened 3-column viewer read cleanly? (ties into the surfaced design call above)** 19 lifetime rows now span two columns (weekly | lifetime | lifetime-cont.) in a 1200-wide panel. Is it legible and uncluttered at the 1280√ó720 scale, do the long tier-status strings ("Titanium ¬∑ 12,431 ‚Üí 25,000") fit without clipping the names, and is the weekly-then-two-lifetime grouping clear ‚Äî or would a scroll / different split read better? All layout numbers are tunable in `drawAchievements`.

**Tiered achievements (v3.0 P7) ‚Äî (the tier/persistence/test logic is headless-solid; everything here is look/feel):**
6a. **Do the tier badges + colours read as ranks, not hazards?** Open Pause ‚Üí Options ‚Üí Achievements and look at the seven tiered lifetime rows. Does the `TIER_COLOR[]` ramp (warm bronze ‚Üí cool white-hot diamond) read as an ascending rank ladder ‚Äî and, crucially, do none of the six badge tints get mistaken for a Hunter/Debris/salvage/enemy tell (FLAG A-1-a)? The pale top three (titanium/platinum/diamond) are the ones to watch; all six are one-line tunables in `TIER_COLOR[]`.
6b. **Does "progress-to-next" make sense at a glance?** Each tiered row reads e.g. "Gold ¬∑ 12,431 ‚Üí 25,000" (badge ¬∑ current ‚Üí next threshold), "Diamond ‚úì MAX" at the ceiling, "‚Äî ¬∑ 0 ‚Üí 1,000" before bronze. Is that legible and self-explanatory next to the single-goal `cur/goal` rows in the same panel, or does the mixed layout read as cluttered?
6c. **Does a big lifetime jump popping several toasts feel good or spammy?** A large delivery/kill session can cross two or three tiers in one `evaluate()` and stack that many ascending, tier-named toasts ("‚Ä¶ ‚Äî Bronze", "‚Ä¶ ‚Äî Silver", "‚Ä¶ ‚Äî Gold"). Does the cascade feel like a satisfying reward, or is it noisy? If spammy, the documented fix is to collapse a multi-crossing into a single "reached Gold" toast.
6d. **(Persistence, ties into ask #1)** Earn a tier, close the tab, reopen ‚Äî does the badge come back? And for a returning player who had the old `afd_achievements_v1` save: do their lifetime counters survive and tier badges recompute (the best-effort `_v1‚Üí_v2` migration, FLAG A-2-a)? Their current-week weekly unlocks may reset once ‚Äî expected.

**Growing tow cap + chain retune (v3.0 P6) (the math + stability are headless-solid; everything here is feel/perf):**
5a. **Does a full max chain feel *heavy but drivable*, not broken?** Grow the cap toward 20 (deliver a lot) and tow a full 20-chain. It's tuned to land on the *old full-12 feel* (~45% thrust / ~63% top speed). Does that read as "a heavy but manageable haul," or does 20 canisters *still* feel broken/whippy despite the retune?
5b. **Is the now-lighter base-12 chain a problem?** Because the per-node penalty shrank, a fresh-run 12-chain is lighter than it used to be (~58% thrust / ~74% top speed / 0.84 tug vs the old 45%/63%/1.4). Does the early game feel *too* floaty when towing, or is the extra early nimbleness fine (you grow into the weight)?
5c. **Does the cap-growth cadence feel *earned*?** +1 per 30 canisters delivered (‚âà240 to reach 20 ‚Äî roughly 8‚Äì16 waves of active hauling). Too slow (never see 20 in a normal run)? Too fast? Does the "TOW +1" float read clearly as "your cap just went up," and does `CARGO n/20` on the HUD make sense?
5d. **Any whip/perf issues at 20 nodes in dense late waves (FLAG B-8-c)?** More towed nodes + the high canister volume = more `shadowBlur`. Watch frame rate towing a long chain through a busy late wave; if it drops, a global glow toggle is the lever (decay is gone as of v3.2 P3 ‚Äî see ask 9f for the permanent-garbage perf watch).

**Difficulty options / powerup expiry modes (v3.0 P5) ‚Äî (default `"time"` = nothing changes (default `"time"` = nothing changes; these all need opting in on Options ‚Üí Difficulty):**
4a. **Do the count budgets feel right?** Turn on **shot powerups = Shots** and play with Rapid/Triple: do 40 rapid pulls / 30 triple pulls read as a fair "use it or lose it" alternative to the 15 s clock, or too stingy / too generous? Same question for **Magnet = Pieces** at 20 canisters hooked.
4b. **Is the count HUD legible?** In a count mode the active-effect bar shows `remaining/budget` with a **numeric** count beside it (instead of a draining timer). Does the number read at a glance during play, and does a count bar sit clearly alongside a *timed* Engine bar when both are up?
4c. **Is the Difficulty screen discoverable and clear?** Pause ‚Üí Options ‚Üí Difficulty. Do the two "Time | Shots" / "Time | Pieces" toggles read unambiguously (‚óÑ = time, ‚ñ∫ = count), and does ‚óÑ/‚ñ∫ flipping them feel right on keyboard **and** gamepad? Does it persist across a reload (same `afd_settings_v1` caveat as F8 ‚Äî real persistence is browser-only)?
4d. **Rapid+Triple independent expiry** ‚Äî with both on in Shots mode, when Triple's 30 runs out first you keep firing *single* shots at rapid cadence until Rapid's 40 is spent. Does that transition read as intended, or confusing?

**Pause / menu from any state + corrected controls (v3.0 P4) (needs a controller for the first two):**
3a. **Does Start-as-session-toggle feel natural on a controller?** One button that starts a game on the title, opens the pause dialog mid-game, and dismisses/resumes while paused ‚Äî does that read as intuitive (the standard console idiom), or do you reach for a separate "pause" and "start"?
3b. **Do "O" (keyboard) and controller "B" read as the options/achievements entry from the title/gameover?** Is it discoverable from the on-screen hint ("OPTIONS / ACHIEVEMENTS: O (controller: B)")? Does opening the system menu, browsing Achievements/Options, and backing out feel clean ‚Äî or does "B to open" fight your instinct that B = cancel?
3c. **Is ESC-vs-B "back" ever ambiguous inside a menu?** ESC and B both mean "back" once a menu is open (and ESC pauses / B opens when no menu is up). Backing out step-by-step (Achievements ‚Üí Options ‚Üí root ‚Üí resume) ‚Äî does it ever feel like a keypress did the wrong thing, or backed out one level too many/few?
3d. **Is retiring "P" for ESC-as-pause the right call (FLAG P4-a)?** P no longer pauses. If muscle memory wants P, say so and it can be re-added as a secondary playing-pause alias.

**Targets-remaining HUD (v3.0 P3):**
2a. **Does `TARGETS n` under CARGO read clearly at a glance during play?** It's a plain number, no icon ‚Äî does it register as "how many things are left" without a legend?
2b. **Does the count *rising* mid-wave read as intended, or as confusing/buggy-looking?** Two ways it can happen: a large Debris splitting (jumps +2 on one kill), and ‚Äî the more likely one to raise an eyebrow ‚Äî a Hunter lineage sliding in on its own timer well after the Debris field looks nearly clear, ticking `TARGETS` back up from a low number. Does that read as "a new threat arrived," or does it feel like the game moved the goalposts? If it's confusing, the documented fallback is splitting the readout into **`DEBRIS n ¬∑ HUNTERS m`** so the Hunter arrival reads as an addition rather than a rewind ‚Äî flag which you'd prefer.
2c. **Is the position (directly under CARGO, powerup row bumped down 20px) crowding the top-left HUD**, especially with 1‚Äì2 active powerup bars also showing?

**Fire-rate rebalance (v3.0 P2):**
-1a. **Does the slower base gun (0.20 s, was 0.16 s) feel sluggish, or is it barely noticeable?** Clear waves 1‚Äì3 at the base cadence (no Rapid Fire picked up) and compare against memory/feel of the old rate. Time it if useful.
-1b. **Does Rapid Fire now feel meaningfully faster**, not just "more bullets allowed"? Pick one up and fire continuously ‚Äî does the cadence bump read as intentional and satisfying?
-1c. **Is Rapid+Triple together too dominant?** It's now the strongest combo by design of this fix (fast cadence + wide spread) ‚Äî flagged as FLAG B-6-a, not yet rebalanced. Does it trivialize waves/Hunters when both are active, or does the 15 s shared duration keep it in check naturally?

**Starfield legibility & parallax (v3.0 P1):**
0a. **Does the field read as brighter/denser without competing with entities?** Compare the title screen and early gameplay against your memory of the old flat, near-invisible field. Does the varied per-star brightness read as a natural starfield rather than noise? Is `STAR_DENSITY=80` a good density, or does it feel sparse/cluttered at the 1280√ó720 viewport?
0b. **Does the parallax layer read as depth, or as a distracting second field?** Thrust/strafe the ship and watch the near (brighter, sparser) layer drift relative to the far layer. Does the 0.5√ó `STAR_PARALLAX_FACTOR` make ship motion legible as "something in the world," or is it too subtle to notice / too strong and busy? Is the near layer's brightness (`STAR_NEAR_BRIGHT_MIN/MAX` 0.55‚Äì1.0) a good contrast against the far layer?
0c. **Any visible seam or tiling artifact in the near layer** as the camera moves, especially near a world-boundary wrap? The near layer is screen-space tiled (not wrap-math), so this is the one thing headless tests can't fully rule out visually ‚Äî the periodicity test only confirms the *math* repeats cleanly, not that it *looks* seamless. All five constants (`STAR_DENSITY`, `STAR_PARALLAX_FACTOR`, `STAR_BRIGHT_MIN/MAX`, `STAR_NEAR_DENSITY`, `STAR_NEAR_BRIGHT_MIN/MAX`) are single-knob tunables.

**World-boundary line (v2.1):**
0. **Does the dotted boundary read clearly, and is it the right brightness?** Fly toward a world edge until the dashed rectangle scrolls into view, then cross it. Does the line clearly say "here's the wrap seam" as you approach *and* as you pass through it (it should sit at screen-center at the moment of crossing)? Is the `COLOR.dim` tone + low glow unobtrusive ‚Äî reads as a boundary, not a hazard/enemy ‚Äî or is it too bright/distracting over a busy field, or conversely too faint to notice? Is the dash density (`BOUNDARY_DASH` 16 / `BOUNDARY_GAP` 24) comfortable at the viewport scale, or does it want longer/shorter dashes? All four `BOUNDARY_*` constants are single-knob tunables. *(Only judgeable in a real browser ‚Äî the headless test confirms the geometry/z-order/no-gameplay-effect, not the look.)*

**Achievements (v2.0/F9):**
1. **Do settings AND achievements actually persist across a real reload?** This is the top ask. Earn an achievement (e.g. deliver 20 canisters ‚Üí Scrap Runner, or destroy 15 debris ‚Üí Satellite Buster), change some volumes/bindings, close the tab, reopen the file. Are the unlock, the lifetime counters, and the settings all still there? Two separate `localStorage` keys are in play (`afd_settings_v1`, **`afd_achievements_v2`** as of P7) ‚Äî confirm both survive, including tier badges (see ask 6d for the `_v1‚Üí_v2` migration). *(Only confirmable outside the artifact sandbox ‚Äî headless tests exercise only the serialize/deserialize logic.)*
2. **Does the unlock toast read clearly and feel good?** Non-blocking gold banner top-centre, ~4.5 s, fade in/out, stacks if several land at once, plus a rising-triad chime. Is it legible over a busy field? Too long/short? Does it distract during intense play (it's drawn on top of everything, including the pause menu)?
3. **Is the Achievements viewer legible?** Pause ‚Üí Options ‚Üí Achievements: this week's 5 (left) + the 12 lifetime (right), each with a ‚úì/`cur/goal`, earned rows in gold. 17 rows in one panel ‚Äî does it feel cramped, and do the progress numbers read at a glance? Would you want a first-class title-screen entry (currently only the hint is there)?
4. **Do the achievement thresholds feel earnable-but-meaningful?** The 27 goals are first-pass from the starter pools. Any that feel unreachable, trivial, or degenerate (Waste Not especially ‚Äî flagged as near-impossible-yet-cheesable)? This decides which to retune/retire in a curation pass.
5. **Sanity-check the "same 5 every week" premise informally** ‚Äî the active weekly set is fixed by the ISO calendar week; it should be stable all week and change on Monday (UTC). No action needed unless it visibly misbehaves.

**Menu / options / rebinding (v1.9/F8):**
6. Does menu navigation feel natural on **keyboard and gamepad** (slider granularity at `VOL_STEP` 0.1; edge-detected one-press-one-move gamepad nav vs. wanting held auto-repeat)?
7. Does a **rebound control take effect immediately** in live play? Are the two quirks acceptable ‚Äî a gamepad rebind **dropping that action's stick axis**, and **no conflict detection** when rebinding to an already-used key?

**Controller (v1.8/F7):** deadzone comfort at `GP_DEADZONE` 0.25; shield on RT/RB (a gap-fill ‚Äî right button?); D-Pad-vs-stick feel; whether a controller-only start produces sound or needs one keyboard press to unlock audio (known Web Audio limitation).

**Powerups (v1.7/F6):** drop rate (`POWERUP_DROP_CHANCE` 0.10) + ambient Health cadence feel *earned but not stingy*; Magnet pull reads as a sweep not a jitter; the five icons + HUD duration row read clearly.

**Hunters (v1.6/F4):** early-game calm at `HUNTER_FLOOR_FRAC` 0.58 vs. a smooth escalation; the point-blank shield-kill of a medium (spawns 3 scattering smalls) feels *fair*, not a death trap.

**Saucers / pacing (v1.5/F10):** waves 1‚Äì4 feel calm; ramp intensity reads as a schedule, not a cliff.

**Salvage / garbage (v1.4/F3 + v1.3):** the field reads as "richly optional salvage," not "carpeted in clutter"; 12 s decay is long enough to collect a lineage without feeling frantic; knockback never yanks the ship somewhere that unfairly severs the whole haul; a fresh wave spawn can't instantly sever a fresh chain too often. **And the deferred joint F3+F10 Debris-density retune** ‚Äî with every system now in, this is the last major early-game balance pass; judge it once the combined field feel is confirmed.
